mūḍhā amitrā nyarbude jahy eṣāṃ varaṃ varam
anayā jahi senayā
yaś ca kavacī yaś cākavaco 'mitro yaś cājmani
jyāpāśaiḥ kavacapāśair ajmanābhihataḥ śayām
ye varmiṇo ye 'varmāṇo amitrā ye ca varmiṇaḥ
sarvāṃs tāṁ arbude hatāṁ chvāno 'dantu bhūmyām
ye rathino ye arathā asādā ye ca sādinaḥ
sarvān adantu tān hatān gṛdhrāḥ śyenāḥ patatriṇaḥ
sahasrakuṇapā śetām āmitrī senā samare vadhānām
vividdhā kakajākṛtā
marmāvidhaṃ roruvataṃ suparṇair adantu duścitaṃ mṛditaṃ śayānam
ya imāṃ pratīcīm āhutim amitro no yuyutsati
yāṃ devā anutiṣṭhanti yasyā nāsti virādhanam
tayendro hantu vṛtrahā vajreṇa triṣandhinā
satyaṃ bṛhad ṛtam ugraṃ dīkṣā tapo brahma yajñaḥ pṛthivīṃ dhārayanti
sā no bhūtasya bhavyasya patny uruṃ lokaṃ pṛthivī naḥ kṛṇotu
asaṃbādhaṃ madhyato mānavānāṃ yasyā udvataḥ pravataḥ samaṃ bahu
nānāvīryā oṣadhīr yā bibharti pṛthivī naḥ prathatāṃ rādhyatāṃ naḥ
yasyāṃ samudra uta sindhur āpo yasyām annaṃ kṛṣṭayaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ
yasyām idaṃ jinvati prāṇad ejat sā no bhūmiḥ pūrvapeye dadhātu
yasyāś catasraḥ pradiśaḥ pṛthivyā yasyām annam kṛṣṭayaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ
yā bibharti bahudhā prāṇad ejat sā no bhūmir goṣv apy anne dadhātu
yasyām pūrve pūrva janāḥ vicakrire yasyām devāḥ asurān abhyavartayan gavām aśvānām vayasaḥ ca viṣṭhā
bhagam varcaḥ pṛthivī naḥ dadhātu
viśvaṃbharā vasu dhānī pratiṣṭhā hiraṇya vakṣāḥ jagataḥ niveśanī vaiśvānaram bibhratī bhūmiḥ agnim indra ṛṣabhā draviṇe naḥ dadhātu
yāṃ rakṣanty asvapnā viśvadānīṃ devā bhūmiṃ pṛthivīm apramādam
sā no madhu priyaṃ duhām atho ukṣatu varcasā
yārṇave 'dhi salilam agra āsīt yāṃ māyābhir anvacaran manīṣiṇaḥ
yasyā hṛdayaṃ parame vyomant satyenāvṛtam amṛtaṃ pṛthivyāḥ
sā no bhūmis tviṣiṃ balaṃ rāṣṭre dadhātūttame
yasyām āpaḥ paricarāḥ samānīr ahorātre apramādaṃ kṣaranti
sā no bhūmir bhūridhārā payo duhām atho ukṣatu varcasā
yām aśvināv amimātāṃ viṣṇur yasyāṃ vicakrame
indro yāṃ cakra ātmane 'namitrāṃ śacīpatiḥ
sā no bhūmir visṛjatāṃ mātā putrāya me payaḥ
girayas te parvatā himavanto 'raṇyaṃ te pṛthivi syonam astu
babhruṃ kṛṣṇāṃ rohiṇīṃ viśvarūpāṃ dhruvāṃ bhūmiṃ pṛthivīm indraguptām
ajīto 'hato akṣato 'dhyaṣṭhām pṛthivīm aham
yat te madhyaṃ pṛthivi yac ca nabhyaṃ yās ta ūrjas tanvaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ
tāsu no dhehy abhi naḥ pavasva mātā bhūmiḥ putro ahaṃ pṛthivyāḥ parjanyaḥ pitā sa u naḥ pipartu
yasyāṃ vediṃ parigṛhṇanti bhūmyāṃ yasyāṃ yajñaṃ tanvate viśvakarmāṇaḥ
yasyāṃ mīyante svaravaḥ pṛthivyām ūrdhvāḥ śukrā āhutyāḥ purastāt
sā no bhūmir vardhayad vardhamānā
yo no dveṣat pṛthivi yaḥ pṛtanyād yo 'bhidāsān manasā yo vadhena
taṃ no bhūme randhaya pūrvakṛtvari
tvaj jātās tvayi caranti martyās tvaṃ bibharṣi dvipadas tvaṃ catuṣpadaḥ
taveme pṛthivi pañca mānavā yebhyo jyotir amṛtaṃ martyebhya udyant sūryo raśmibhir ātanoti
tā naḥ prajāḥ saṃ duhratāṃ samagrā vāco madhu pṛthivi dhehi mahyam
viśvasvaṃ mātaram oṣadhīnāṃ dhruvāṃ bhūmiṃ pṛthivīṃ dharmaṇā dhṛtām
śivāṃ syonām anu carema viśvahā
mahat sadhasthaṃ mahatī babhūvitha mahān vega ejathur vepathuṣ ṭe
mahāṃs tvendro rakṣaty apramādam
sā no bhūme prarocaya hiraṇyasyeva saṃdṛśi mā no dvikṣata kaścana
agnir bhūmyām oṣadhīṣv agnim āpo bibhraty agnir aśmasu
agnir antaḥ puruṣeṣu goṣv aśveṣv agnayaḥ
agnir diva ātapaty agner devasyorv antarikṣam
agniṃ martāsa indhate havyavāhaṃ ghṛtapriyam
agnivāsāḥ pṛthivy asitajñūs tviṣīmantaṃ saṃśitaṃ mā kṛṇotu
bhūmyāṃ devebhyo dadati yajñaṃ havyam araṃkṛtam
bhūmyāṃ manuṣyā jīvanti svadhayānnena martyāḥ
sā no bhūmiḥ prāṇam āyur dadhātu jaradaṣṭiṃ mā pṛthivī kṛṇotu
yas te gandhaḥ pṛthivi saṃbabhūva yaṃ bibhraty oṣadhayo yam āpaḥ
yaṃ gandharvā apsarasaś ca bhejire tena mā surabhiṃ kṛṇu mā no dvikṣata kaścana
yas te gandhaḥ puṣkaram āviveśa yaṃ saṃjabhruḥ sūryāyā vivāhe
amartyāḥ pṛthivi gandham agre tena mā surabhiṃ kṛṇu mā no dvikṣata kaścana
yas te gandhaḥ puruṣeṣu strīṣu puṃsu bhago ruciḥ
yo aśveṣu vīreṣu yo mṛgeṣūta hastiṣu
kanyāyāṃ varco yad bhūme tenāsmāṁ api saṃsṛja mā no dvikṣata kaścana
śilā bhūmir aśmā pāṃsuḥ sā bhūmiḥ saṃdhṛtā dhṛtā
tasyai hiraṇyavakṣase pṛthivyā akaraṃ namaḥ
yasyāṃ vṛkṣā vānaspatyā dhruvās tiṣṭhanti viśvahā
pṛthivīṃ viśvadhāyasaṃ dhṛtām acchāvadāmasi
udīrāṇā utāsīnās tiṣṭhantaḥ prakrāmantaḥ
padbhyāṃ dakṣiṇasavyābhyāṃ mā vyathiṣmahi bhūmyām
vimṛgvarīṃ pṛthivīm āvadāmi kṣamāṃ bhūmiṃ brahmaṇā vāvṛdhānām
ūrjaṃ puṣṭaṃ bibhratīm annabhāgaṃ ghṛtaṃ tvābhiniṣīdema bhūme
śuddhā na āpas tanve kṣarantu yo naḥ syedur apriye taṃ nidadhmaḥ
pavitreṇa pṛthivi motpunāmi
yās te prācīḥ pradiśo yā udīcīr yās te bhūme adharād yāś ca paścāt
syonās tā mahyaṃ carate bhavantu mā nipaptaṃ bhuvane śiśriyāṇaḥ
mā naḥ paścān mā purastān nudiṣṭhā mottarād adharād uta
svasti bhūme no bhava mā vidan paripanthino varīyo yāvayā vadham
yāvat te 'bhi vipaśyāmi bhūme sūryeṇa medinā
tāvan me cakṣur mā meṣṭottarāmuttarāṃ samām
yac chayānaḥ paryāvarte dakṣiṇaṃ savyam abhi bhūme pārśvam uttānās tvā pratīcīṃ yat pṛṣṭībhir adhiśemahe
mā hiṃsīs tatra no bhūme sarvasya pratiśīvari
yat te bhūme vikhanāmi kṣipraṃ tad apirohatu
mā te marma vimṛgvari mā te hṛdayam arpipam
grīṣmas te bhūme varṣāṇi śaraddhemantaḥ śiśiro vasantaḥ
ṛtavas te vihitā hāyanīr ahorātre pṛthivi no duhātām
yāpa sarpaṃ vijamānā vimṛgvarī yasyām āsann agnayo ye apsv antaḥ
parā dasyūn dadatī devapīyūn indraṃ vṛṇānā pṛthivī na vṛtram śakrāya dadhre vṛṣabhāya vṛṣṇe
yasyāṃ sadohavirdhāne yūpo yasyāṃ nimīyate
brahmāṇo yasyām arcanty ṛgbhiḥ sāmnā yajurvidaḥ yujyante yasyām ṛtvijaḥ somam indrāya pātave
yasyāṃ pūrve bhūtakṛta ṛṣayo gā udānṛcchuḥ
sapta satreṇa vedhaso yajñena tapasā saha
sā no bhūmir ādiśatu yad dhanaṃ kāmayāmahe
bhago anuprayuṅktām indra etu purogavaḥ
yasyāṃ gāyanti nṛtyanti bhūmyāṃ martyā vyailabāḥ
yudhyante yasyām ākrando yasyām vadati dundubhiḥ
sā no bhūmiḥ praṇudatāṃ sapatnān asapatnaṃ mā pṛthivī kṛṇotu
yasyām annaṃ vrīhiyavau yasyā imāḥ pañca kṛṣṭayaḥ
bhūmyai parjanyapatnyai namo 'stu varṣamedase
yasyāḥ puro devakṛtāḥ kṣetre yasyā vikurvate
prajāpatiḥ pṛthivīṃ viśvagarbhām āśāmāśāṃ raṇyāṃ naḥ kṛṇotu
nidhiṃ bibhratī bahudhā guhā vasu maṇiṃ hiraṇyaṃ pṛthivī dadātu me
vasūni no vasudā rāsamānā devī dadhātu sumanasyamānā
janaṃ bibhratī bahudhā vivācasaṃ nānādharmāṇaṃ pṛthivī yathaukasam
sahasraṃ dhārā draviṇasya me duhāṃ dhruveva dhenur anapasphurantī
yas te sarpo vṛścikas tṛṣṭadaṃśmā hemantajabdho bhṛmalo guhā śaye
krimir jinvat pṛthivi yadyad ejati prāvṛṣi tan naḥ sarpan mopasṛpad yac chivaṃ tena no mṛḍa
ye te panthāno bahavo janāyanā rathasya vartmānasaś ca yātave
yaiḥ saṃcaranty ubhaye bhadrapāpās taṃ panthānaṃ jayemānamitram ataskaraṃ yac chivaṃ tena no mṛḍa
malvaṃ bibhratī gurubhṛd bhadrapāpasya nidhanaṃ titikṣuḥ
varāheṇa pṛthivī saṃvidānā sūkarāya vijihīte mṛgāya
ye ta āraṇyāḥ paśavo mṛgā vane hitāḥ siṃhā vyāghrāḥ puruṣādaś caranti
ulaṃ vṛkaṃ pṛthivi ducchunām ita ṛkṣīkāṃ rakṣo apabādhayāsmat
ye gandharvā apsaraso ye cārāyāḥ kimīdinaḥ
piśācānt sarvā rakṣāṃsi tān asmad bhūme yāvaya
yāṃ dvipādaḥ pakṣiṇaḥ saṃpatanti haṃsāḥ suparṇāḥ śakunā vayāṃsi
yasyāṃ vāto mātariśveyate rajāṃsi kṛṇvaṃś cyāvayaṃś ca vṛkṣān
vātasya pravām upavām anuvāty arciḥ
yasyāṃ kṛṣṇam aruṇaṃ ca saṃhite ahorātre vihite bhūmyām adhi
varṣeṇa bhūmiḥ pṛthivī vṛtāvṛtā sā no dadhātu bhadrayā priye dhāmani dhāmani
dyauś ca ma idaṃ pṛthivī cāntarikṣaṃ ca me vyacaḥ
agniḥ sūrya āpo medhāṃ viśve devāś ca saṃdaduḥ
aham asmi sahamāna uttaro nāma bhūmyām
abhīṣāḍ asmi viśvāṣāḍ āśāmāśāṃ viṣāsahiḥ
ado yad devi prathamānā purastād devair uktā vyasarpo mahitvam
ā tvā subhūtam aviśat tadānīm akalpayathāḥ pradiśaś catasraḥ
ye grāmā yad araṇyaṃ yāḥ sabhā adhi bhūmyām
ye saṃgrāmāḥ samitayas teṣu cāru vadema te
aśva iva rajo dudhuve vi tān janān ya ākṣiyan pṛthivīṃ yād ajāyata
mandrāgretvarī bhuvanasya gopā vanaspatīnāṃ gṛbhir oṣadhīnām
yad vadāmi madhumat tad vadāmi yad īkṣe tad vananti mā
tviṣīmān asmi jūtimān avānyān hanmi dodhataḥ
śantivā surabhiḥ syonā kīlālodhnī payasvatī
bhūmir adhibravītu me pṛthivī payasā saha
yām anvaicchaddhaviṣā viśvakarmāntar arṇave rajasi praviṣṭām
bhujiṣyaṃ pātraṃ nihitaṃ guhā yad āvir bhoge abhavan mātṛmadbhyaḥ
tvam asy āvapanī janānām aditiḥ kāmadughā paprathānā
yat ta ūnaṃ tat ta āpūrayāti prajāpatiḥ prathamajā ṛtasya
upasthāḥ te anamīvāḥ ayakṣmāḥ asmabhyam santu pṛthivi prasūtāḥ
dīrgham naḥ āyuḥ pratibudhyamānāḥ vayam tubhyam bali hṛtaḥ syāma
bhūme mātar nidhehi mā bhadrayā supratiṣṭhitam
saṃvidānā divā kave śriyāṃ mā dhehi bhūtyām
naḍam āroha na te atra loka idaṃ sīsaṃ bhāgadheyaṃ ta ehi
yo goṣu yakṣmaḥ puruṣeṣu yakṣmas tena tvaṃ sākam adharāṅ parehi
aghaśaṃsaduḥśaṃsābhyāṃ kareṇānukareṇa ca
yakṣmaṃ ca sarvaṃ teneto mṛtyuṃ ca nirajāmasi
nir ito mṛtyuṃ nirṛtiṃ nir arātim ajāmasi
yo no dveṣṭi tam addhy agne akravyād yam u dviṣmas tam u te prasuvāmasi
yady agniḥ kravyād yadi vā vyāghra imaṃ goṣṭhaṃ praviveśānyokāḥ
taṃ māṣājyaṃ kṛtvā prahiṇomi dūraṃ sa gacchatv apsuṣado 'py agnīn
yat tvā kruddhāḥ pracakrur manyunā puruṣe mṛte
sukalpam agne tat tvayā punas tvoddīpayāmasi
punas tvādityā rudrā vasavaḥ punar brahmā vasunītir agne
punas tvā brahmaṇaspatir ādhād dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya
yo agniḥ kravyāt praviveśa no gṛham imaṃ paśyann itaraṃ jātavedasam
taṃ harāmi pitṛyajñāya dūraṃ sa gharmam indhāṃ parame sadhasthe
kravyādam agniṃ prahiṇomi dūram yamarājño gacchatu ripravāhaḥ
ihāyam itaro jātavedā devo devebhyo havyaṃ vahatu prajānan
kravyādam agnim iṣito harāmi janān dṛṃhantaṃ vajreṇa mṛtyum
ni taṃ śāsmi gārhapatyena vidvān pitṝṇāṃ loke 'pi bhāgo astu
kravyādam agniṃ śaśamānam ukthyaṃ prahiṇomi pathibhiḥ pitṛyāṇaiḥ
mā devayānaiḥ punar āgā atraivaidhi pitṛṣu jāgṛhi tvam
samindhate saṃkasukaṃ svastaye śuddhā bhavantaḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ
jahāti ripram aty ena eti samiddho agniḥ supunā punāti
devo agniḥ saṃkasuko divas pṛṣṭhāny āruhat
mucyamāno nir enaso 'mog asmāṁ aśastyāḥ
asmin vayaṃ saṃkasuke agnau riprāṇi mṛjmahe
abhūma yajñiyāḥ śuddhāḥ pra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣat
saṃkasuko vikasuko nirṛtho yaś ca nisvaraḥ
te te yakṣmaṃ savedaso dūrād dūram anīnaśan
yo no aśveṣu vīreṣu yo no goṣv ajāviṣu
kravyādaṃ nirṇudāmasi yo agnir janayopanaḥ
anyebhyas tvā puruṣebhyo gobhyo aśvebhyas tvā
niḥ kravyādaṃ nudāmasi yo agnir jīvitayopanaḥ
yasmin devā amṛjata yasmin manuṣyā uta
tasmin ghṛtastāvo mṛṣṭvā tvam agne divaṃ ruha
samiddho agna āhuta sa no mābhyapakramīḥ
atraiva dīdihi dyavi jyok ca sūryaṃ dṛśe
sīse mṛḍḍhvaṃ naḍe mṛḍḍhvam agnau saṃkasuke ca yat
atho avyāṃ rāmāyāṃ śīrṣaktim upabarhaṇe
sīse malaṃ sādayitvā śīrṣaktim upabarhaṇe
avyām asiknyāṃ mṛṣṭvā śuddhā bhavata yajñiyāḥ
paraṃ mṛtyo anu parehi panthāṃ yas ta eṣa itaro devayānāt
cakṣuṣmate śṛṇvate te bravīmīheme vīrā bahavo bhavantu
ime jīvā vi mṛtair āvavṛtrann abhūd bhadrā devahutir no adya
prāñco agāma nṛtaye hasāya suvīrāso vidatham ā vadema
imaṃ jīvebhyaḥ paridhiṃ dadhāmi maiṣāṃ nu gād aparo artham etam
śataṃ jīvantaḥ śaradaḥ purūcīs tiro mṛtyuṃ dadhatām parvatena
ārohatāyur jarasaṃ vṛṇānā anupūrvaṃ yatamānā yati stha
tān vas tvaṣṭā sujanimā sajoṣāḥ sarvam āyur nayatu jīvanāya
yathāhāny anupūrvaṃ bhavanti yathartava ṛtubhir yanti sākam
yathā na pūrvam aparo jahāty evā dhātar āyūṃṣi kalpayaiṣām
aśmanvatī rīyate saṃrabhadhvaṃ vīrayadhvaṃ pra taratā sakhāyaḥ
atrā jahīta ye asan durevā anamīvān ut taremābhi vājān
uttiṣṭhatā prataratā sakhāyo 'śmanvatī nadī syandata iyam
atrā jahīta ye asann aśivāḥ śivānt syonān ut taremābhi vājān
vaiśvadevīṃ varcasā ārabhadhvaṃ śuddhā bhavantaḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ
atikrāmanto duritā padāni śataṃ himāḥ sarvavīrā madema
udīcīnaiḥ pathibhir vāyumadbhir atikrāmanto 'varān parebhiḥ
triḥ sapta kṛtvarṣayaḥ paretā mṛtyuṃ pratyauhan padayopanena
mṛtyoḥ padaṃ yopayanta eta drāghīya āyuḥ prataraṃ dadhānāḥ
āsīnā mṛtyuṃ nudatā sadhasthe 'tha jīvāso vidatham āvadema
imā nārīr avidhavāḥ supatnīr āñjanena sarpiṣā saṃspṛśantām
anaśravo anamīvāḥ suratnā ārohantu janayo yonim agre
vyākaromi haviṣāham etau tau brahmaṇā vy ahaṃ kalpayāmi
svadhāṃ pitṛbhyo ajarāṃ kṛṇomi dīrgheṇāyuṣā sam imānt sṛjāmi
yo no agniḥ pitaro hṛtsv antar āviveśāmṛto martyeṣu
mayy ahaṃ taṃ parigṛhṇāmi devaṃ mā so asmān dvikṣata mā vayaṃ tam
apāvṛtya gārhapatyāt kravyādā preta dakṣiṇā
priyaṃ pitṛbhya ātmane brahmabhyaḥ kṛṇutā priyam
dvibhāgadhanam ādāya prakṣiṇāty avartyā
agniḥ putrasya jyeṣṭhasya yaḥ kravyād anirāhitaḥ
yat kṛṣate yad vanute yac ca vasnena vindate
sarvaṃ martyasya tan nāsti kravyāc ced anirāhitaḥ
a yajñiyaḥ hata varcāḥ bhavati
na enena haviḥ attave
chinatti kṛṣyā gor dhanād yaṃ kravyād anuvartate
muhur gṛdhyaiḥ pravadaty ārtim martyo nītya
kravyād yān agnir antikād anuvidvān vitāvati
grāhyā gṛhāḥ saṃsṛjyante striyā yan mriyate patiḥ
brahmaiva vidvān eṣyo yaḥ kravyādaṃ nirādadhat
yad ripraṃ śamalaṃ cakṛma yac ca duṣkṛtam
āpo mā tasmācchumbhantvagneḥ saṃkasukāc ca yat
tā adharād udīcīr āvavṛtran prajānatīḥ pathibhir devayānaiḥ
parvatasya vṛṣabhasyādhi pṛṣṭhe navāś caranti saritaḥ purāṇīḥ
agne akravyān niḥ kravyādaṃ nudā devayajanaṃ vaha
imaṃ kravyād āviveśāyaṃ kravyādam anvagāt
vyāghrau kṛtvā nānānaṃ taṃ harāmi śivāparam
antardhir devānāṃ paridhir manuṣyāṇām agnir gārhapatya ubhayān antarā śritaḥ
jīvānām āyuḥ pratira tvam agne pitṝṇāṃ lokam api gacchantu ye mṛtāḥ
sugārhapatyo vitapann arātim uṣāmuṣāṃ śreyasīṃ dhehy asmai
sarvān agne sahamānaḥ sapatnān aiṣām ūrjaṃ rayim asmāsu dhehi
imam indraṃ vahniṃ paprim anvārabhadhvaṃ sa vo nirvakṣad duritād avadyāt
tenāpahata śarum āpatantaṃ tena rudrasya paripātāstām
anaḍvāhaṃ plavam anvārabhadhvaṃ sa vo nirvakṣad duritād avadyāt
ārohata savitur nāvam etāṃ ṣaḍbhir urvībhir amatiṃ tarema
ahorātre anveṣi bibhrat kṣemyas tiṣṭhan prataraṇaḥ suvīraḥ
anāturānt sumanasas talpa bibhraj jyog eva naḥ puruṣagandhir edhi
te devebhya āvṛścante pāpaṃ jīvanti sarvadā
kravyād yān agnir antikād aśva ivānuvapate naḍam
ye 'śraddhā dhanakāmyā kravyādā samāsate
te vā anyeṣāṃ kumbhīṃ paryādadhati sarvadā
preva pipatiṣati manasā muhur āvartate punaḥ
kravyād yān agnir antikād anuvidvān vitāvati
aviḥ kṛṣṇā bhāgadheyaṃ paśūnāṃ sīsaṃ kravyād api candraṃ ta āhuḥ
māṣāḥ piṣṭā bhāgadheyaṃ te havyam araṇyānyā gahvaraṃ sacasva
iṣīkāṃ jaratīm iṣṭvā tilpiñjaṃ daṇḍanaṃ naḍam
tam indra idhmam kṛtvā yamasyāgniṃ nirādadhau
pratyañcam arkaṃ pratyarpayitvā pravidvān panthāṃ vi hy āviveśa
parāmīṣām asūn dideśa dīrgheṇāyuṣā sam imānt sṛjāmi
pumān puṃso 'dhitiṣṭha carmehi tatra hvayasva yatamā priyā te
yāvantāv agre prathamaṃ sameyathus tad vāṃ vayo yamarājye samānam
tāvad vāṃ cakṣus tati vīryāṇi tāvat tejas tatidhā vājināni
agniḥ śarīraṃ sacate yadaidho 'dhā pakvān mithunā saṃbhavāthaḥ
sam asmiṃlloke sam u devayāne saṃ smā sametaṃ yamarājyeṣu
pūtau pavitrair upa taddhvayethāṃ yadyad reto adhi vāṃ saṃbabhūva
āpas putrāso abhisaṃviśadhvam imaṃ jīvaṃ jīvadhanyāḥ sametya
tāsāṃ bhajadhvam amṛtaṃ yam āhur odanaṃ pacati vāṃ janitrī
yaṃ vāṃ pitā pacati yaṃ ca mātā riprān nirmuktyai śamalāc ca vācaḥ
sa odanaḥ śatadhāraḥ svarga ubhe vyāpa nabhasī mahitvā
ubhe nabhasī ubhayāṃś ca lokān ye yajvanām abhijitāḥ svargāḥ
teṣāṃ jyotiṣmān madhumān yo agre tasmin putrair jarasi saṃśrayethām
prācīṃ prācīṃ pradiśam ārabhethām etaṃ lokaṃ śraddadhānāḥ sacante
yad vāṃ pakvaṃ pariviṣṭam agnau tasya guptaye daṃpatī saṃśrayethām
dakṣiṇāṃ diśam abhi nakṣamāṇau paryāvartethām abhi pātram etat
tasmin vāṃ yamaḥ pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ pakvāya śarma bahulaṃ niyacchāt
pratīcī diśām iyam id varaṃ yasyāṃ somo adhipā mṛḍitā ca
tasyāṃ śrayethāṃ sukṛtaḥ sacethām adhā pakvān mithunā saṃbhavāthaḥ
uttaraṃ rāṣṭraṃ prajayottarāvad diśām udīcī kṛṇavan no agram
pāṅktaṃ chandaḥ puruṣo babhūva viśvair viśvāṅgaiḥ saha sambhavema
dhruveyaṃ virāṇ namo astv asyai śivā putrebhya uta mahyam astu
sā no devy adite viśvavāra irya iva gopā abhirakṣa pakvam
piteva putrān abhisaṃsvajasva naḥ śivā no vātā iha vāntu bhūmau
yam odanaṃ pacato devate iha taṃ nas tapa uta satyaṃ ca vettu
yad yat kṛṣṇaḥ śakuna eha gatvā tsaran viṣaktaṃ bila āsasāda
yad vā dāsy ārdrahastā samaṅkta ulūkhalaṃ musalaṃ śumbhatāpaḥ
ayaṃ grāvā pṛthubudhno vayodhāḥ pūtaḥ pavitrair apahantu rakṣaḥ
āroha carma mahi śarma yaccha mā daṃpatī pautram aghaṃ nigātām
vanaspatiḥ saha devair na āgan rakṣaḥ piśācāṁ apabādhamānaḥ
sa ucchrayātai pravadāti vācaṃ tena lokāṁ abhi sarvān jayema
sapta medhān paśavaḥ paryagṛhṇan ya eṣāṃ jyotiṣmāṁ uta yaś cakarśa
trayastriṃśad devatās tānt sacante sa naḥ svargam abhi neṣa lokam
svargaṃ lokam abhi no nayāsi saṃ jāyayā saha putraiḥ syāma
gṛhṇāmi hastam anu maitv atra mā nas tārīn nirṛtir mo arātiḥ
grāhiṃ pāpmānam ati tāṁ ayāma tamo vyasya pravadāsi valgu
vānaspatya udyato mā jihiṃsīr mā taṇḍulaṃ viśarīr devayantam
viśvavyacā ghṛtapṛṣṭho bhaviṣyant sayonir lokam upayāhy etam
varṣavṛddham upayaccha śūrpaṃ tuṣaṃ palāvān apa tad vinaktu
trayo lokāḥ saṃmitā brāhmaṇena dyaur evāsau pṛthivy antarikṣam
aṃśūn gṛbhītvānvārabhethām āpyāyantāṃ punar āyantu śūrpam
pṛthag rūpāṇi bahudhā paśūnām ekarūpo bhavasi saṃ samṛddhyā
etāṃ tvacaṃ lohinīṃ tāṃ nudasva grāvā śumbhāti malaga iva vastrā
pṛthivīṃ tvā pṛthivyām āveśayāmi tanūḥ samānī vikṛtā ta eṣā
yadyad dyuttaṃ likhitam arpaṇena tena mā susror brahmaṇāpi tad vapāmi
janitrīva pratiharyāsi sūnuṃ saṃ tvā dadhāmi pṛthivīṃ pṛthivyā
ukhā kumbhī vedyāṃ mā vyathiṣṭhā yajñāyudhair ājyenātiṣaktā
agniḥ pacan rakṣatu tvā purastād indro rakṣatu dakṣiṇato marutvān
varuṇas tvā dṛṃhāddharuṇe pratīcyā uttarāt tvā somaḥ saṃdadātai
pūtāḥ pavitraiḥ pavante abhrād divaṃ ca yanti pṛthivīṃ ca lokān
tā jīvalā jīvadhanyāḥ pratiṣṭhāḥ pātra āsiktāḥ pary agnir indhām
āyanti divaḥ pṛthivīṃ sacante bhūmyāḥ sacante adhy antarikṣam
śuddhāḥ satīs tā u śumbhanta eva tā naḥ svargam abhi lokaṃ nayantu
uteva prabhvīr uta saṃmitāsa uta śukrāḥ śucayaś cāmṛtāsaḥ
tā odanaṃ daṃpatibhyāṃ praśiṣṭā āpaḥ śikṣantīḥ pacatā sunāthāḥ
saṃkhyātā stokāḥ pṛthivīṃ sacante prāṇāpānaiḥ saṃmitā oṣadhībhiḥ
asaṃkhyātā opyamānāḥ suvarṇāḥ sarvaṃ vyāpuḥ śucayaḥ śucitvam
udyodhanty abhivalganti taptāḥ phenam asyanti bahulāṃś ca bindūn
yoṣeva dṛṣṭvā patim ṛtviyāyaitais taṇḍulair bhavatā sam āpaḥ
utthāpaya sīdato budhna enān adbhir ātmānam abhisaṃspṛśantām
amāsi pātrair udakaṃ yad etan mitās taṇḍulāḥ pradiśo yadīmāḥ
prayaccha parśuṃ tvarayā harauṣam ahiṃsanta oṣadhīr dāntu parvan
yāsāṃ somaḥ pari rājyaṃ babhūvāmanyutā no vīrudho bhavantu
navaṃ barhir odanāya stṛṇīta priyaṃ hṛdaś cakṣuṣo valgv astu
tasmin devāḥ saha daivīr viśantv imaṃ prāśnantv ṛtubhir niṣadya
vanaspate stīrṇam āsīda barhir agniṣṭomaiḥ saṃmito devatābhiḥ
tvaṣṭreva rūpaṃ sukṛtaṃ svadhityainā ehāḥ pari pātre dadṛśrām
ṣaṣṭyāṃ śaratsu nidhipā abhīcchāt svaḥ pakvenābhyaśnavātai
upainaṃ jīvān pitaraś ca putrā etaṃ svargaṃ gamayāntam agneḥ
dhartā dhriyasva dharuṇe pṛthivyā acyutaṃ tvā devatāś cyāvayantu
taṃ tvā daṃpatī jīvantau jīvaputrāv udvāsayātaḥ pary agnidhānāt
sarvānt samāgā abhijitya lokān yāvantaḥ kāmāḥ samatītṛpas tān
vigāhethām āyavanaṃ ca darvir ekasmin pātre adhy uddharainam
upastṛṇīhi prathaya purastād ghṛtena pātram abhighārayaitat
vāśrevosrā taruṇaṃ stanasyum imaṃ devāso abhihiṅkṛṇota
upāstarīr akaro lokam etam uruḥ prathatām asamaḥ svargaḥ
tasmiṃchrayātai mahiṣaḥ suparṇo devā enaṃ devatābhyaḥ prayacchān
yadyaj jāyā pacati tvat paraḥ paraḥ patir vā jāye tvat tiraḥ
saṃ tat sṛjethāṃ saha vāṃ tad astu sampādayantau saha lokam ekam
yāvanto asyāḥ pṛthivīṃ sacante asmat putrāḥ pari ye saṃbabhūvuḥ
sarvāṃs tāṁ upa pātre hvayethāṃ nābhiṃ jānānāḥ śiśavaḥ samāyān
vasor yā dhārā madhunā prapīnā ghṛtena miśrā amṛtasya nābhayaḥ
sarvās tā avarundhe svargaḥ ṣaṣṭyāṃ śaratsu nidhipā abhīcchāt
nidhiṃ nidhipā abhy enam icchād anīśvarā abhitaḥ santu ye 'nye
asmābhir datto nihitaḥ svargas tribhiḥ kāṇḍais trīnt svargān arukṣat
agnī rakṣas tapatu yad videvaṃ kravyād piśāca iha mā prapāsta
nudāma enam aparudhmo asmad ādityā enam aṅgirasaḥ sacantām
ādityebhyo aṅgirobhyo madhv idaṃ ghṛtena miśraṃ prativedayāmi
śuddhahastau brāhmaṇasyānihatyaitaṃ svargaṃ sukṛtāv apītam
idaṃ prāpam uttamaṃ kāṇḍam asya yasmāl lokāt parameṣṭhī samāpa
āsiñca sarpir ghṛtavat samaṅgdhy eṣa bhāgo aṅgiraso no atra
satyāya ca tapase devatābhyo nidhiṃ śevadhiṃ paridadma etam
mā no dyūte 'vagān mā samityāṃ mā smānyasmā utsṛjatā purā mat
ahaṃ pacāmy ahaṃ dadāmi mamed u karman karuṇe 'dhi jāyā
kaumāro loko ajaniṣṭa putro 'nvārabhethāṃ vaya uttarāvat
na kilbiṣam atra nādhāro asti na yan mitraiḥ samamamāna eti
anūnaṃ pātraṃ nihitaṃ na etat paktāraṃ pakvaḥ punar āviśāti
priyaṃ priyāṇāṃ kṛṇavāma tamas te yantu yatame dviṣanti
dhenur anaḍvān vayo vaya āyad eva pauruṣeyam apa mṛtyuṃ nudantu
sam agnayaḥ vidur anyo anyaṃ ya oṣadhīḥ sacate yaś ca sindhūn
yāvanto devā divy ātapanti hiraṇyaṃ jyotiḥ pacato babhūva
eṣā tvacāṃ puruṣe saṃbabhūvānagnāḥ sarve paśavo ye anye
kṣatreṇātmānaṃ paridhāpayātho 'motaṃ vāso mukham odanasya
yad akṣeṣu vadā yat samityāṃ yad vā vadā anṛtaṃ vittakāmyā
samānaṃ tantum abhisaṃvasānau tasmint sarvaṃ śamalaṃ sādayāthaḥ
varṣaṃ vanuṣvāpigaccha devāṃs tvaco dhūmaṃ paryutpātayāsi
viśvavyacā ghṛtapṛṣṭho bhaviṣyant sayonir lokam upayāhy etam
tanvaṃ svargo bahudhā vicakre yathā vida ātmann anyavarṇām
apājait kṛṣṇāṃ ruśatīṃ punāno yā lohinī tāṃ te agnau juhomi
prācyai tvā diśe 'gnaye 'dhipataye 'sitāya rakṣitra ādityāyeṣumate
etaṃ paridadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ
diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase nineṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha sambhavema
dakṣiṇāyai tvā diśa indrāyādhipataye tiraścirājaye rakṣitre yamāyeṣumate
etaṃ paridadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ
diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase nineṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha sambhavema
pratīcyai tvā diśe varuṇāyādhipataye pṛdākave rakṣitre 'nnāyeṣumate
etaṃ paridadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ
diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase nineṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha sambhavema
udīcyai tvā diśe somāyādhipataye svajāya rakṣitre 'śanyā iṣumatyai
etaṃ paridadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ
diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase nineṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha sambhavema
dhruvāyai tvā diśe viṣṇave 'dhipataye kalmāṣagrīvāya rakṣitra oṣadhībhya iṣumatībhyaḥ
etaṃ paridadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ
diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase nineṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha sambhavema
ūrdhvāyai tvā diśe bṛhaspataye 'dhipataye śvitrāya rakṣitre varṣāyeṣumate
etaṃ paridadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ
diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase nineṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha sambhavema
dadāmīty eva brūyād anu cainām abhutsata
vaśāṃ brahmabhyo yācadbhyas tat prajāvad apatyavat
prajayā sa vikrīṇīte paśubhiś copadasyati
ya ārṣeyebhyo yācadbhyo devānāṃ gāṃ na ditsati
kūṭayāsya saṃśīryante śloṇayā kāṭam ardati
baṇḍayā dahyante gṛhāḥ kāṇayā dīyate svam
vilohito adhiṣṭhānācchakno vindati gopatim
tathā vaśāyāḥ saṃvidyaṃ duradabhnā hy ucyase
pador asyā adhiṣṭhānād viklindur nāma vindati
anāmanāt saṃśīryante yā mukhenopajighrati
yo asyāḥ karṇāv āskunoty ā sa deveṣu vṛścate
lakṣma kurva iti manyate kanīyaḥ kṛṇute svam
yad asyāḥ kasmaicid bhogāya bālān kaścit prakṛntati
tataḥ kiśorā mriyante vatsāṃś ca ghātuko vṛkaḥ
yad asyā gopatau satyā loma dhvāṅkṣo ajīhiḍat
tataḥ kumārā mriyante yakṣmo vindaty anāmanāt
yad asyāḥ palpūlanaṃ śakṛd dāsī samasyati
tato 'parūpaṃ jāyate tasmād avyeṣyad enasaḥ
jāyamānābhijāyate devānt sabrāhmaṇān vaśā
tasmād brahmabhyo deyaiṣā tad āhuḥ svasya gopanam
ya enāṃ vanim āyanti teṣāṃ devakṛtā vaśā
brahmajyeyaṃ tad abruvan ya enāṃ nipriyāyate
ya ārṣeyebhyo yācadbhyo devānāṃ gāṃ na ditsati
ā sa deveṣu vṛścate brāhmaṇānāṃ ca manyave
yo asya syād vaśābhogo anyām iccheta tarhi saḥ
hiṃste adattā puruṣaṃ yācitāṃ ca na ditsati
yathā śevadhir nihito brāhmaṇānāṃ tathā vaśā
tām etad acchāyanti yasmin kasmiṃś ca jāyate
svam etad acchāyanti yad vaśāṃ brāhmaṇā abhi
yathainān anyasmin jinīyād evāsyā nirodhanam
cared evā traihāyaṇād avijñātagadā satī
vaśāṃ ca vidyān nārada brāhmaṇās tarhy eṣyāḥ
ya enām avaśām āha devānāṃ nihitaṃ nidhim
ubhau tasmai bhavāśarvau parikramyeṣum asyataḥ
yo asyā ūdho na vedātho asyā stanān uta
ubhayenaivāsmai duhe dātuṃ ced aśakad vaśām
duradabhnainam āśaye yācitāṃ ca na ditsati
nāsmai kāmāḥ samṛdhyante yām adattvā cikīrṣati
devā vaśām ayācan mukhaṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇam
teṣāṃ sarveṣām adadaddheḍaṃ nyeti mānuṣaḥ
heḍaṃ paśūnāṃ nyeti brāhmaṇebhyo 'dadad vaśām
devānāṃ nihitaṃ bhāgaṃ martyaś cen nipriyāyate
yad anye śataṃ yāceyur brāhmaṇā gopatiṃ vaśām
athaināṃ devā abruvann evaṃ ha viduṣo vaśā
ya evaṃ viduṣe 'dattvāthānyebhyo dadad vaśām
durgā tasmā adhiṣṭhāne pṛthivī sahadevatā
devā vaśām ayācan yasminn agre ajāyata
tām etāṃ vidyān nāradaḥ saha devair udājata
anapatyam alpapaśuṃ vaśā kṛṇoti pūruṣam
brāhmaṇaiś ca yācitām athaināṃ nipriyāyate
agnīṣomābhyāṃ kāmāya mitrāya varuṇāya ca
tebhyo yācanti brāhmaṇās teṣv āvṛścate 'dadat
yāvad asyā gopatir nopaśṛṇuyād ṛcaḥ svayam
cared asya tāvad goṣu nāsya śrutvā gṛhe vaset
yo asyā ṛca upaśrutyātha goṣv acīcarat
āyuś ca tasya bhūtiṃ ca devā vṛścanti hīḍitāḥ
vaśā carantī bahudhā devānāṃ nihito nidhiḥ
āviṣkṛṇuṣva rūpāṇi yadā sthāma jighāṃsati
āvir ātmānaṃ kṛṇute yadā sthāma jighāṃsati
atho ha brahmabhyo vaśā yāñcyāya kṛṇute manaḥ
manasā saṃkalpayati tad devāṁ apigacchati
tato ha brahmāṇo vaśām upaprayanti yācitum
svadhākāreṇa pitṛbhyo yajñena devatābhyaḥ
dānena rājanyo vaśāyā mātur heḍam na gacchati
vaśā mātā rājanyasya tathā sambhūtam agraśaḥ
tasyā āhur anarpaṇaṃ yad brahmabhyaḥ pradīyate
yathājyaṃ pragṛhītam ālumpet sruco agnaye
evā ha brahmabhyo vaśām agnaya āvṛścate 'dadat
puroḍāśavatsā sudughā loke 'smā upatiṣṭhati
sā asmai sarvān kāmān vaśā pradaduṣe duhe
sarvān kāmān yama rājye vaśā pradaduṣe duhe
athāhur nārakaṃ lokaṃ nirundhānasya yācitām
pravīyamānā carati kruddhā gopataye vaśā
vehataṃ mā manyamāno mṛtyoḥ pāśeṣu badhyatām
yo vehataṃ manyamāno 'mā ca pacate vaśām
apy asya putrān pautrāṃś ca yācayate bṛhaspatiḥ
mahad eṣāvatapati carantī goṣu gaur api
atho ha gopataye vaśādaduṣe viṣaṃ duhe
priyaṃ paśūnāṃ bhavati yad brahmabhyaḥ pradīyate
atho vaśāyās tat priyaṃ yad devatrā haviḥ syāt
yā vaśā udakalpayan devā yajñād udetya
tāsāṃ viliptyaṃ bhīmām udākuruta nāradaḥ
tāṃ devā amīmāṃsanta vaśeyā3m avaśeti
tām abravīn nārada eṣā vaśānāṃ vaśatameti
kati nu vaśā nārada yās tvaṃ vettha manuṣyajāḥ
tās tvā pṛcchāmi vidvāṃsaṃ kasyā nāśnīyād abrāhmaṇaḥ
viliptyā bṛhaspate yā ca sūtavaśā vaśā
tasyā nāśnīyād abrāhmaṇo ya āśaṃseta bhūtyām
namas te astu nāradānuṣṭhu viduṣe vaśā
katamāsāṃ bhīmatamā yām adattvā parābhavet
viliptī yā bṛhaspate 'tho sūtavaśā vaśā
tasyā nāśnīyād abrāhmaṇo ya āśaṃseta bhūtyām
trīṇi vai vaśājātāni viliptī sūtavaśā vaśā
tāḥ prayacched brahmabhyaḥ so 'nāvraskaḥ prajāpatau
etad vo brāhmaṇā havir iti manvīta yācitaḥ
vaśāṃ ced enaṃ yāceyur yā bhīmādaduṣo gṛhe
devā vaśāṃ paryavadan na no 'dād iti hīḍitāḥ
etābhir ṛgbhir bhedaṃ tasmād vai sa parābhavat
utaināṃ bhedo nādadād vaśām indreṇa yācitaḥ
tasmāt taṃ devā āgaso 'vṛścann ahamuttare
ye vaśāyā adānāya vadanti parirāpiṇaḥ
indrasya manyave jālmā āvṛścante acittyā
ye gopatiṃ parāṇīyāthāhur mā dadā iti
rudrasyāstāṃ te hetiṃ pariyanty acittyā
yadi hutāṃ yady ahutām amā ca pacate vaśām
devānt sabrāhmaṇān ṛtvā jihmo lokān nirṛcchati
śrameṇa tapasā sṛṣṭā brahmaṇā vittarte śritā
satyenāvṛtā śriyā prāvṛtā yaśasā parīvṛtā
svadhayā parihitā śraddhayā paryūḍhā dīkṣayā guptā yajñe pratiṣṭhitā loko nidhanam
brahma padavāyaṃ brāhmaṇo 'dhipatiḥ
tām ādadānasya brahmagavīṃ jinato brāhmaṇaṃ kṣatriyasya
apakrāmati sūnṛtā vīryaṃ puṇyā lakṣmīḥ
ojaś ca tejaś ca sahaś ca balaṃ ca vāk cendriyaṃ ca śrīś ca dharmaś ca
brahma ca kṣatraṃ ca rāṣṭraṃ ca viśaś ca tviṣiś ca yaśaś ca varcaś ca draviṇaṃ ca
āyuś ca rūpaṃ ca nāma ca kīrtiś ca prāṇaś cāpānaś ca cakṣuś ca śrotraṃ ca
payaś ca rasaś cānnaṃ cānnādyaṃ cartaṃ ca satyaṃ ceṣṭaṃ ca pūrtaṃ ca prajā ca paśavaś ca
tāni sarvāṇy apakrāmanti brahmagavīm ādadānasya jinato brāhmaṇaṃ kṣatriyasya
saiṣā bhīmā brahmagavy aghaviṣā sākṣāt kṛtyā kūlbajam āvṛtā
sarvāṇy asyāṃ ghorāṇi sarve ca mṛtyavaḥ
sarvāṇy asyāṃ krūrāṇi sarve puruṣavadhāḥ
sā brahmajyaṃ devapīyuṃ brahmagavy ādīyamānā mṛtyoḥ paḍbīśa ādyati
meniḥ śatavadhā hi sā brahmajyasya kṣitir hi sā
tasmād vai brāhmaṇānāṃ gaur durādharṣā vijānatā
vajro dhāvantī vaiśvānara udvītā
hetiḥ śaphān utkhidantī mahādevo 'pekṣamāṇā
kṣurapavir īkṣamāṇā vāśyamānābhisphūrjati
mṛtyur hiṃkṛṇvaty ugro devaḥ pucchaṃ paryasyantī
sarvajyāniḥ karṇau varīvarjayantī rājayakṣmo mehantī
menir duhyamānā śīrṣaktir dugdhā
sedir upatiṣṭhantī mithoyodhaḥ parāmṛṣṭā
śaravyā mukhe 'pinahyamānartir hanyamānā
aghaviṣā nipatantī tamo nipatitā
anugacchantī prāṇān upadāsayati brahmagavī brahmajyasya
vairaṃ vikṛtyamānā pautrādyaṃ vibhājyamānā
devahetir hriyamāṇā vyṛddhir hṛtā
pāpmādhidhīyamānā pāruṣyam avadhīyamānā
viṣaṃ prayasyantī takmā prayastā
aghaṃ pacyamānā duṣvapnyaṃ pakvā
mūlabarhaṇī paryākriyamāṇā kṣitiḥ paryākṛtā
asaṃjñā gandhena śug uddhriyamāṇāśīviṣa uddhṛtā
abhūtir upahriyamāṇā parābhūtir upahṛtā
śarvaḥ kruddhaḥ piśyamānā śimidā piśitā
avartir aśyamānā nirṛtir aśitā
aśitā lokāc chinatti brahmagavī brahmajyam asmāc cāmuṣmāc ca
tasyā āhananaṃ kṛtyā menir āśasanaṃ valaga ūbadhyam
asvagatā parihṇutā
agniḥ kravyād bhūtvā brahmagavī brahmajyaṃ praviśyātti
sarvāsyāṅgā parvā mūlāni vṛścati
chinatty asya pitṛbandhu parābhāvayati mātṛbandhu
vivāhāṁ jñātīnt sarvān apikṣāpayati brahmagavī brahmajyasya kṣatriyeṇāpunardīyamānā
avāstum enam asvagam aprajasaṃ karoty aparāparaṇo bhavati kṣīyate
ya evaṃ viduṣo brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyo gām ādatte
kṣipraṃ vai tasyāhanane gṛdhrāḥ kurvata ailabam
kṣipraṃ vai tasyādahanaṃ parinṛtyanti keśinīr āghnānāḥ pāṇinorasi kurvāṇāḥ pāpam ailabam
kṣipraṃ vai tasya vāstuṣu vṛkāḥ kurvata ailabam
kṣipraṃ vai tasya pṛcchanti yat tad āsī3d idaṃ nu tā3d iti
chinddhy āchinddhi prachinddhy apikṣāpaya kṣāpaya
ādadānam āṅgirasi brahmajyam upadāsaya
vaiśvadevī hy ucyase kṛtyā kūlbajam āvṛtā
oṣantī samoṣantī brahmaṇo vajraḥ
kṣurapavir mṛtyur bhūtvā vidhāva tvam
ādatse jinatāṃ varca iṣṭaṃ pūrtaṃ cāśiṣaḥ
ādāya jītaṃ jītāya loke 'muṣmin prayacchasi
aghnye padavīr bhava brāhmaṇasyābhiśastyā
meniḥ śaravyā bhavāghād aghaviṣā bhava
aghnye pra śiro jahi brahmajyasya kṛtāgaso devapīyor arādhasaḥ
tvayā pramūrṇaṃ mṛditam agnir dahatu duścitam
vṛśca pravṛśca saṃvṛśca daha pradaha saṃdaha
brahmajyaṃ devy aghnya ā mūlād anusaṃdaha
yathāyād yamasādanāt pāpalokān parāvataḥ
evā tvaṃ devy aghnye brahmajyasya kṛtāgaso devapīyor arādhasaḥ
vajreṇa śataparvaṇā tīkṣṇena kṣurabhṛṣṭinā
pra skandhān pra śiro jahi
lomāny asya saṃchinddhi tvacam asya viveṣṭaya
māṃsāny asya śātaya snāvāny asya saṃvṛha
asthīny asya pīḍaya majjānam asya nirjahi
sarvāsyāṅgā parvāṇi viśrathaya
agnir enaṃ kravyāt pṛthivyā nudatām udoṣatu vāyur antarikṣān mahato varimṇaḥ
sūrya enaṃ divaḥ praṇudatāṃ nyoṣatu
udehi vājin yo apsv antar idaṃ rāṣṭraṃ praviśa sūnṛtāvat
yo rohito viśvam idaṃ jajāna sa tvā rāṣṭrāya subhṛtaṃ bibhartu
ud vāja āgan yo apsv antar viśa āroha tvadyonayo yāḥ
somaṃ dadhāno 'pa oṣadhīr gāś catuṣpado dvipada āveśayeha
yūyam ugrā marutaḥ pṛśnimātara indreṇa yujā pramṛṇīta śatrūn
ā vo rohitaḥ śṛṇavat sudānavas triṣaptāso marutaḥ svādusaṃmudaḥ
ruho ruroha rohita āruroha garbho janīnāṃ januṣām upastham
tābhiḥ saṃrabdham anvavindan ṣaḍ urvīr gātuṃ prapaśyann iha rāṣṭram āhāḥ
ā te rāṣṭram iha rohito 'hārṣīd vyāsthan mṛdho abhayaṃ te abhūt
tasmai te dyāvāpṛthivī revatībhiḥ kāmaṃ duhātām iha śakvarībhiḥ
rohito dyāvāpṛthivī jajāna tatra tantuṃ parameṣṭhī tatāna
tatra śiśriye 'ja ekapādo 'dṛṃhad dyāvāpṛthivī balena
rohito dyāvāpṛthivī adṛṃhat tena sva stabhitaṃ tena nākaḥ
tenāntarikṣaṃ vimitā rajāṃsi tena devā amṛtam anvavindan
vi rohito amṛśad viśvarūpaṃ samākurvāṇaḥ praruho ruhaś ca
divaṃ rūḍhvā mahatā mahimnā saṃ te rāṣṭram anaktu payasā ghṛtena
yās te ruhaḥ praruho yās ta āruho yābhir āpṛṇāsi divam antarikṣam
tāsāṃ brahmaṇā payasā vavṛdhāno viśi rāṣṭre jāgṛhi rohitasya
yās te viśas tapasaḥ saṃbabhūvur vatsaṃ gāyatrīm anu tā ihāguḥ
tās tvā viśantu manasā śivena saṃmātā vatso abhyetu rohitaḥ
ūrdhvo rohito adhi nāke asthād viśvā rūpāṇi janayan yuvā kaviḥ
tigmenāgnir jyotiṣā vibhāti tṛtīye cakre rajasi priyāṇi
sahasraśṛṅgo vṛṣabho jātavedā ghṛtāhutaḥ somapṛṣṭhaḥ suvīraḥ
mā mā hāsīn nāthito net tvā jahāni gopoṣaṃ ca me vīrapoṣaṃ ca dhehi
rohito yajñasya janitā mukhaṃ ca rohitāya vācā śrotreṇa manasā juhomi
rohitaṃ devā yanti sumanasyamānāḥ sa mā rohaiḥ sāmityai rohayatu
rohito yajñaṃ vyadadhād viśvakarmaṇe tasmāt tejāṃsy upa memāny āguḥ
voceyaṃ te nābhiṃ bhuvanasyādhi majmani
ā tvā ruroha bṛhaty uta paṅktir ā kakub varcasā jātavedaḥ
ā tvā rurohoṣṇihākṣaro vaṣaṭkāra ā tvā ruroha rohito retasā saha
ayaṃ vaste garbhaṃ pṛthivyā divaṃ vaste 'yam antarikṣam
ayaṃ bradhnasya viṣṭapi svar lokān vyānaśe
vācaspate pṛthivī naḥ syonā syonā yonis talpā naḥ suśevā
ihaiva prāṇaḥ sakhye no astu taṃ tvā parameṣṭhin pary agnir āyuṣā varcasā dadhātu
vācaspata ṛtavaḥ pañca ye nau vaiśvakarmaṇāḥ pari ye saṃbabhūvuḥ
ihaiva prāṇaḥ sakhye no astu taṃ tvā parameṣṭhin pari rohita āyuṣā varcasā dadhātu
vācaspate saumanasaṃ manaś ca goṣṭhe no gā janaya yoniṣu prajāḥ
ihaiva prāṇaḥ sakhye no astu taṃ tvā parameṣṭhin pary aham āyuṣā varcasā dadhātu
pari tvā dhāt savitā devo agnir varcasā mitrāvaruṇāv abhi tvā
sarvā arātīr avakrāmann ehīdaṃ rāṣṭram akaraḥ sūnṛtāvat
yaṃ tvā pṛṣatī rathe praṣṭir vahati rohita
śubhā yāsi riṇann apaḥ
anuvratā rohiṇī rohitasya sūriḥ suvarṇā bṛhatī suvarcāḥ
tayā vājān viśvarūpāṁ jayema tayā viśvāḥ pṛtanā abhiṣyāma
idaṃ sado rohiṇī rohitasyāsau panthāḥ pṛṣatī yena yāti
tāṃ gandharvāḥ kaśyapā unnayanti tāṃ rakṣanti kavayo 'pramādam
sūryasyāśvā harayaḥ ketumantaḥ sadā vahanty amṛtāḥ sukhaṃ ratham
ghṛtapāvā rohito bhrājamāno divaṃ devaḥ pṛṣatīm āviveśa
yo rohito vṛṣabhas tigmaśṛṅgaḥ pary agniṃ pari sūryaṃ babhūva
yo viṣṭabhnāti pṛthivīṃ divaṃ ca tasmād devā adhi sṛṣṭīḥ sṛjante
rohito divam āruhan mahataḥ pary arṇavāt
sarvā ruroha rohito ruhaḥ
vimimīṣva payasvatīṃ ghṛtācīṃ devānāṃ dhenur anapaspṛg eṣā
indraḥ somaṃ pibatu kṣemo astv agniḥ prastautu vi mṛdho nudasva
samiddho agniḥ samidhāno ghṛtavṛddho ghṛtāhutaḥ
abhīṣāṭ viśvāṣāḍ agniḥ sapatnān hantu ye mama
hantv enān pradahatv arir yo naḥ pṛtanyati
kravyādāgninā vayaṃ sapatnān pradahāmasi
avācīnān avajahīndra vajreṇa bāhumān
adhā sapatnān māmakān agnes tejobhir ādiṣi
agne sapatnān adharān pādayāsmad vyathayā sajātam utpipānaṃ bṛhaspate
indrāgnī mitrāvaruṇāv adhare padyantām apratimanyūyamānāḥ
udyaṃs tvaṃ deva sūrya sapatnān ava me jahi
avainān aśmanā jahi te yantv adhamaṃ tamaḥ
vatso virājo vṛṣabho matīnām āruroha śukrapṛṣṭho 'ntarikṣam
ghṛtenārkam abhyarcanti vatsaṃ brahma santaṃ brahmaṇā vardhayanti
divaṃ ca roha pṛthivīṃ ca roha rāṣṭraṃ ca roha draviṇaṃ ca roha
prajāṃ ca rohāmṛtaṃ ca roha rohitena tanvaṃ saṃspṛśasva
ye devā rāṣṭrabhṛto 'bhito yanti sūryam
taiṣ ṭe rohitaḥ saṃvidāno rāṣṭraṃ dadhātu sumanasyamānaḥ
ut tvā yajñā brahmapūtā vahanty adhvagato harayas tvā vahanti
tiraḥ samudram ati rocase 'rṇavam
rohite dyāvāpṛthivī adhiśrite vasujiti gojiti saṃdhanājiti
sahasraṃ yasya janimāni sapta ca voceyaṃ te nābhiṃ bhuvanasyādhi majmani
yaśā yāsi pradiśo diśaś ca yaśāḥ paśūnām uta carṣaṇīnām
yaśāḥ pṛthivyāḥ adityāḥ upasthe aham bhūyāsam savitā iva cāruḥ
amutra sann iha vetthetaḥ saṃs tāni paśyasi
itaḥ paśyanti rocanaṃ divi sūryaṃ vipaścitam
devo devān marcayasy antaś carasy arṇave
samānam agnim indhate taṃ viduḥ kavayaḥ pare
avaḥ pareṇa para enāvareṇa padā vatsaṃ bibhratī gaur udasthāt
sā kadrīcī kaṃ svid ardhaṃ parāgāt kva svit sūte nahi yūthe asmin
ekapadī dvipadī sā catuṣpady aṣṭāpadī navapadī babhūvuṣī
sahasrākṣarā bhuvanasya paṅktis tasyāḥ samudrā adhi vikṣaranti
ārohan dyām amṛtaḥ prāva me vacaḥ
ut tvā yajñā brahmapūtā vahanty adhvagato harayas tvā vahanti
veda tat te amartya yat ta ākramaṇaṃ divi
yat te sadhasthaṃ parame vyoman
sūryo dyāṃ sūryaḥ pṛthivīṃ sūrya āpo 'tipaśyati
sūryo bhūtasyaikaṃ cakṣur āruroha divaṃ mahīm
urvīr āsan paridhayo vedir bhūmir akalpata
tatraitāv agnī ādhatta himaṃ ghraṃsaṃ ca rohitaḥ
himaṃ ghraṃsaṃ cādhāya yūpān kṛtvā parvatān
varṣājyāv agnī ījāte rohitasya svarvidaḥ
svarvido rohitasya brahmaṇāgniḥ samidhyate
tasmādghraṃsas tasmāddhimas tasmād yajño 'jāyata
brahmaṇāgnī vāvṛdhānau brahmavṛddhau brahmāhutau
brahmeddhāv agnī ījāte rohitasya svarvidaḥ
satye anyaḥ samāhito 'psv anyaḥ samidhyate
brahmeddhāv agnī ījāte rohitasya svarvidaḥ
yaṃ vātaḥ pariśumbhati yaṃ vendro brahmaṇaspatiḥ
brahmeddhāvagnī ījāte rohitasya svarvidaḥ
vediṃ bhūmiṃ kalpayitvā divaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇām
ghraṃsaṃ tad agniṃ kṛtvā cakāra viśvam ātmanvad varṣeṇājyena rohitaḥ
varṣam ājyaṃ ghraṃso agnir vedir bhūmir akalpata
tatraitān parvatān agnir gīrbhir ūrdhvāṁ akalpayat
gīrbhir ūrdhvān kalpayitvā rohito bhūmim abravīt
tvayīdaṃ sarvaṃ jāyatāṃ yad bhūtaṃ yac ca bhāvyam
sa yajñaḥ prathamo bhūto bhavyo ajāyata
tasmāddha jajña idaṃ sarvaṃ yat kiṃcedaṃ virocate rohitena ṛṣiṇābhṛtam
yaś ca gāṃ padā sphurati pratyaṅ sūryaṃ ca mehati
tasya vṛścāmi te mūlaṃ na chāyāṃ karavo 'param
yo mābhichāyam atyeṣi māṃ cāgniṃ cāntarā
tasya vṛścāmi te mūlaṃ na chāyāṃ karavo 'param
yo adya deva sūrya tvāṃ ca māṃ cāntarāyati
duṣvapnyaṃ tasmiṃchamalaṃ duritāni ca mṛjmahe
mā pragāma patho vayaṃ mā yajñād indra sominaḥ
mānta sthur no arātayaḥ
yo yajñasya prasādhanas tantur deveṣv ātataḥ
tam āhutam aśīmahi
ud asya ketavo divi śukrā bhrājanta īrate
ādityasya nṛcakṣaso mahivratasya mīḍhuṣaḥ
diśāṃ prajñānāṃ svarayantam arciṣā supakṣam āśuṃ patayantam arṇave
stavāma sūryaṃ bhuvanasya gopāṃ yo raśmibhir diśa ābhāti sarvāḥ
yat prāṅ pratyaṅ svadhayā yāsi śībhaṃ nānārūpe ahanī karṣi māyayā
tad āditya mahi tat te mahi śravo yad eko viśvaṃ pari bhūma jāyase
vipaścitaṃ taraṇiṃ bhrājamānaṃ vahanti yaṃ haritaḥ sapta bahvīḥ
srutād yam atrir divam unnināya taṃ tvā paśyanti pariyāntam ājim
mā tvā dabhan pariyāntam ājiṃ svasti durgāṁ ati yāhi śībham
divaṃ ca sūrya pṛthivīṃ ca devīm ahorātre vimimāno yad eṣi
svasti te sūrya carase rathāya yenobhāv antau pariyāsi sadyaḥ
yaṃ te vahanti harito vahiṣṭhāḥ śatam aśvā yadi vā sapta bahvīḥ
sukhaṃ sūrya ratham aṃśumantaṃ syonaṃ suvahnim adhitiṣṭha vājinam
yaṃ te vahanti harito vahiṣṭhāḥ śatam aśvā yadi vā sapta bahvīḥ
sapta sūryo harito yātave rathe hiraṇyatvacaso bṛhatīr ayukta
amoci śukro rajasaḥ parastād vidhūya devas tamo divam āruhat
ut ketunā bṛhatā deva āgann apāvṛk tamo 'bhi jyotir aśrait
divyaḥ suparṇaḥ sa vīro vyakhyad aditeḥ putro bhuvanāni viśvā
udyan raśmīn ātanuṣe viśvā rūpāṇi puṣyasi
ubhā samudrau kratunā vibhāsi sarvāṃllokān paribhūr bhrājamānaḥ
pūrvāparaṃ carato māyayaitau śiśū krīḍantau pariyāto 'rṇavam
viśvānyo bhuvanā vicaṣṭe hairaṇyair anyaṃ harito vahanti
divi tvāttrir adhārayat sūryā māsāya kartave
sa eṣi sudhṛtas tapan viśvā bhūtāvacākaśat
ubhāv antau samarṣasi vatsaḥ saṃmātarāv iva
nanv etad itaḥ purā brahma devā amī viduḥ
yat samudram anu śritaṃ tat siṣāsati sūryaḥ
adhvāsya vitato mahān pūrvaś cāparaś ca yaḥ
taṃ samāpnoti jūtibhis tato nāpacikitsati
tenāmṛtasya bhakṣaṃ devānāṃ nāvarundhate
ud u tyaṃ jātavedasaṃ devaṃ vahanti ketavaḥ
dṛśe viśvāya sūryam
apa tye tāyavo yathā nakṣatrā yanty aktubhiḥ
sūrāya viśvacakṣase
adṛśrann asya ketavo vi raśmayo janāṁ anu
bhrājanto agnayo yathā
taraṇir viśvadarśato jyotiṣkṛd asi sūrya
viśvam ābhāsi rocana
pratyaṅ devānāṃ viśaḥ pratyaṅṅ udeṣi mānuṣīḥ
pratyaṅ viśvaṃ svar dṛśe
yenā pāvaka cakṣasā bhuraṇyantaṃ janāṁ anu
tvaṃ varuṇa paśyasi
vi dyām eṣi rajas pṛthv ahar mimāno aktubhiḥ
paśyan janmāni sūrya
sapta tvā harito rathe vahanti deva sūrya
śociṣkeśaṃ vicakṣaṇam
ayukta sapta śundhyuvaḥ sūro rathasya naptyaḥ
tābhir yāti svayuktibhiḥ
rohito divam āruhat tapasā tapasvī
sa yonim aiti sa u jāyate punaḥ sa devānām adhipatir babhūva
yo viśvacarṣaṇir uta viśvatomukho yo viśvataspāṇir uta viśvataspṛthaḥ
saṃ bāhubhyāṃ bharati saṃ patatrair dyāvāpṛthivī janayan deva ekaḥ
ekapād dvipado bhūyo vicakrame dvipāt tripādam abhyeti paścāt
dvipāddha ṣaṭpado bhūyo vicakrame ta ekapadas tanvaṃ samāsate
atandro yāsyan harito yad āsthād dve rūpe kṛṇute rocamānaḥ
ketumān udyant sahamāno rajāṃsi viśvā āditya pravato vibhāsi
baṇ mahāṁ asi sūrya baḍ āditya mahāṁ asi
mahāṃs te mahato mahimā tvam āditya mahāṁ asi
rocase divi rocase antarikṣe pataṅga pṛthivyāṃ rocase rocase apsv antaḥ
ubhā samudrau rucyā vyāpitha devo devāsi mahiṣaḥ svarjit
arvāṅ parastāt prayato vyadhva āśur vipaścit patayan pataṅgaḥ
viṣṇur vicittaḥ śavasādhitiṣṭhan pra ketunā sahate viśvam ejat
citraś cikitvān mahiṣaḥ suparṇa ārocayan rodasī antarikṣam
ahorātre pari sūryaṃ vasāne prāsya viśvā tirato vīryāṇi
tigmo vibhrājan tanvaṃ śiśāno 'raṃgamāsaḥ pravato rarāṇaḥ
jyotiṣmān pakṣī mahiṣo vayodhā viśvā āsthāt pradiśaḥ kalpamānaḥ
citraṃ devānām ketur anīkaṃ jyotiṣmān pradiśaḥ sūrya udyan
divākaro 'ti dyumnais tamāṃsi viśvātārīd duritāni śukraḥ
citraṃ devānām udagād anīkaṃ cakṣur mitrasya varuṇasyāgneḥ
āprād dyāvāpṛthivī antarikṣaṃ sūrya ātmā jagatas tasthuṣaś ca
uccā patantam aruṇaṃ suparṇaṃ madhye divas taraṇiṃ bhrājamānam
paśyāma tvā savitāraṃ yam āhur ajasraṃ jyotir yad avindad attriḥ
divas pṛṣṭhe dhāvamānaṃ suparṇam adityāḥ putraṃ nāthakāma upayāmi bhītaḥ
sa naḥ sūrya pratira dīrgham āyur mā riṣāma sumatau te syāma
sahasrāhṇyaṃ viyatāv asya pakṣau harer haṃsasya patataḥ svargam
sa devānt sarvān urasy upadadya saṃpaśyan yāti bhuvanāni viśvā
rohitaḥ kālo abhavad rohito 'gre prajāpatiḥ
rohito yajñānāṃ mukhaṃ rohitaḥ svar ābharat
rohito loko abhavad rohito 'tyatapad divam
rohito raśmibhir bhūmiṃ samudram anusaṃcarat
sarvā diśaḥ samacarad rohito 'dhipatir divaḥ
divaṃ samudram ād bhūmiṃ sarvaṃ bhūtaṃ virakṣati
ārohañchukro bṛhatīr atandro dve rūpe kṛṇute rocamānaḥ
citraś cikitvān mahiṣo vātamāyā yāvato lokān abhi yad vibhāti
abhy anyad eti pary anyad asyate 'horātrābhyāṃ mahiṣaḥ kalpamānaḥ
sūryaṃ vayaṃ rajasi kṣiyantaṃ gātuvidaṃ havāmahe nādhamānāḥ
pṛthivīpro mahiṣo nādhamānasya gātur adabdhacakṣuḥ pari viśvaṃ babhūva
viśvaṃ saṃpaśyant suvidatro yajatra idaṃ śṛṇotu yad ahaṃ bravīmi
pary asya mahimā pṛthivīṃ samudraṃ jyotiṣā vibhrājan pari dyām antarikṣam
sarvaṃ saṃpaśyant suvidatro yajatra idaṃ śṛṇotu yad ahaṃ bravīmi
abodhy agniḥ samidhā janānāṃ prati dhenum ivāyatīm uṣasam
yahvā iva pra vayām ujjihānāḥ pra bhānavaḥ sisrate nākam accha

tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
ekapād dvipado bhūyo vicakrame dvipāt tripādam abhyeti paścāt
catuṣpāc cakre dvipadām abhisvare saṃpaśyan paṅktim upatiṣṭhamānaḥ
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
kṛṣṇāyāḥ putro arjuno rātryā vatso 'jāyata
sa ha dyām adhirohati ruho ruroha rohitaḥ
sa eti savitā svar divas pṛṣṭhe 'vacākaśat
raśmibhir nabha ābhṛtaṃ mahendra ety āvṛtaḥ
sa dhātā sa vidhartā sa vāyur nabha ucchritam
so 'ryamā sa varuṇaḥ sa rudraḥ sa mahādevaḥ
so agniḥ sa u sūryaḥ sa u eva mahāyamaḥ
taṃ vatsā upatiṣṭhanty ekaśīrṣāṇo yutā daśa
paścāt prāñca ātanvanti yad udeti vibhāsati
tasyaiṣa māruto gaṇaḥ sa eti śikyākṛtaḥ
raśmibhir nabha ābhṛtaṃ mahendra ety āvṛtaḥ
tasyeme nava kośā viṣṭambhā navadhā hitāḥ
sa prajābhyo vipaśyati yac ca prāṇati yac ca na
tam idaṃ nigataṃ sahaḥ sa eṣa eka ekavṛd eka eva
ete asmin devā ekavṛto bhavanti
kīrtiś ca yaśaś cāmbhaś ca nabhaś ca brāhmaṇavarcasaṃ cānnaṃ cānnādyaṃ ca
ya etaṃ devam ekavṛtaṃ veda
na dvitīyo na tṛtīyaś caturtho nāpy ucyate
na pañcamo na ṣaṣṭhaḥ saptamo nāpy ucyate
nāṣṭamo na navamo daśamo nāpy ucyate
sa sarvasmai vipaśyati yac ca prāṇati yac ca na
tam idaṃ nigataṃ sahaḥ sa eṣa eka ekavṛd eka eva
sarve asmin devā ekavṛto bhavanti
brahma ca tapaś ca kīrtiś ca yaśaś cāmbhaś ca nabhaś ca brāhmaṇavarcasaṃ cānnaṃ cānnādyaṃ ca
bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca śraddhā ca ruciś ca svargaś ca svadhā ca
ya etaṃ devam ekavṛtaṃ veda
sa eva mṛtyuḥ so 'mṛtaṃ so 'bhvaṃ sa rakṣaḥ
sa rudro vasuvanir vasudeye namovāke vaṣaṭkāro 'nu saṃhitaḥ
tasyeme sarve yātava upa praśiṣam āsate
tasyāmū sarvā nakṣatrā vaśe candramasā saha
sa vā ahno 'jāyata tasmād ahar ajāyata
sa vai rātryā ajāyata tasmād rātrir ajāyata
sa vā antarikṣād ajāyata tasmād antarikṣam ajāyata
sa vai vāyor ajāyata tasmād vāyur ajāyata
sa vai divo 'jāyata tasmād dyaur adhi ajāyata
sa vai digbhyo 'jāyata tasmād diśo 'jāyanta
sa vai bhūmer ajāyata tasmād bhūmir ajāyata
sa vā agner ajāyata tasmād agnir ajāyata
sa vā adbhyo 'jāyata tasmād āpo 'jāyanta
sa vā ṛgbhyo 'jāyata tasmād ṛco 'jāyanta
sa vai yajñād ajāyata tasmād yajño 'jāyata
sa yajñas tasya yajñaḥ sa yajñasya śiraḥ kṛtam
sa stanayati sa vidyotate sa u aśmānam asyati
pāpāya vā bhadrāya vā puruṣāyāsurāya vā
yad vā kṛṇoṣy oṣadhīr yad vā varṣasi bhadrayā yad vā janyam avīvṛdhaḥ
tāvāṃs te maghavan mahimopo te tanvaḥ śatam
upo te baddhe baddhāni yadi vāsi nyarbudam
bhūyān indro namurād bhūyān indrāsi mṛtyubhyaḥ
bhūyān arātyāḥ śacyāḥ patis tvam indrāsi vibhūḥ prabhūr iti tvopāsmahe vayam
namas te astu paśyata paśya mā paśyata
annādyena yaśasā tejasā brāhmaṇavarcasena
ambho amo mahaḥ saha iti tvopāsmahe vayam
ambho aruṇaṃ rajataṃ rajaḥ saha iti tvopāsmahe vayam
uruḥ pṛthuḥ subhūr bhuva iti tvopāsmahe vayam
pratho varo vyaco loka iti tvopāsmahe vayam
bhavadvasur idadvasuḥ saṃyadvasur āyadvasur iti tvopāsmahe vayam
namas te astu paśyata paśya mā paśyata
annādyena yaśasā tejasā brāhmaṇavarcasena
satyenottabhitā bhūmiḥ sūryeṇottabhitā dyauḥ
ṛtenādityās tiṣṭhanti divi somo adhiśritaḥ
somenādityā balinaḥ somena pṛthivī mahī
atho nakṣatrāṇām eṣām upasthe soma āhitaḥ
somaṃ manyate papivān yat sampiṃṣanty oṣadhim
somaṃ yaṃ brahmāṇo vidur na tasyāśnāti pārthivaḥ
yat tvā soma prapibanti tata āpyāyase punaḥ
vāyuḥ somasya rakṣitā samānāṃ māsa ākṛtiḥ
āchadvidhānair gupito bārhataiḥ soma rakṣitaḥ
grāvṇām icchṛṇvan tiṣṭhasi na te aśnāti pārthivaḥ
cittir ā upabarhaṇaṃ cakṣur ā abhyañjanam
dyaur bhūmiḥ kośa āsīd yad ayāt sūryā patim
raibhy āsīd anudeyī nārāśaṃsī nyocanī
sūryāyā bhadram id vāso gāthayaiti pariṣkṛtā
stomā āsan pratidhayaḥ kurīraṃ chanda opaśaḥ
sūryāyā aśvinā varāgnir āsīt purogavaḥ
somo vadhūyur abhavad aśvināstām ubhā varā
sūryāṃ yat patye śaṃsantīṃ manasā savitādadāt
mano asyā ana āsīd dyaur āsīd uta chadiḥ
śukrāv anaḍvāhāv āstāṃ yad ayāt sūryā patim
ṛksāmābhyām abhihitau gāvau te sāmanāv aitām
śrotre te cakre āstāṃ divi panthāś carācaraḥ
śucī te cakre yātyā vyāno akṣa āhataḥ
ano manasmayaṃ sūryārohat prayatī patim
sūryāyā vahatuḥ prāgāt savitā yam avāsṛjat
maghāsu hanyante gāvaḥ phalgunīṣu vyuhyate
yad aśvinā pṛcchamānāv ayātaṃ tricakreṇa vahatuṃ sūryāyāḥ
kvaikaṃ cakraṃ vām āsīt kva deṣṭrāya tasthathuḥ
yad ayātaṃ śubhas patī vareyaṃ sūryām upa
viśve devā anu tad vām ajānan putraḥ pitaram avṛṇīta pūṣā
dve te cakre sūrye brahmāṇa ṛtuthā viduḥ
athaikaṃ cakraṃ yad guhā tad addhātaya id viduḥ
aryamaṇaṃ yajāmahe subandhuṃ pativedanam
urvārukam iva bandhanāt preto muñcāmi nāmutaḥ
preto muñcāmi nāmutaḥ subaddhām amutas karam
yatheyam indra mīḍhvaḥ suputrā subhagāsati
pra tvā muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśād yena tvābadhnāt savitā suśevāḥ
ṛtasya yonau sukṛtasya loke syonaṃ te astu sahasaṃbhalāyai
bhagas tveto nayatu hastagṛhyāśvinā tvā pravahatāṃ rathena
gṛhān gaccha gṛhapatnī yathāso vaśinī tvaṃ vidatham āvadāsi
iha priyaṃ prajāyai te samṛdhyatām asmin gṛhe gārhapatyāya jāgṛhi
enā patyā tanvaṃ saṃspṛśasvātha jivrir vidatham āvadāsi
ihaiva staṃ mā viyauṣṭaṃ viśvam āyur vyaśnutam
krīḍantau putrair naptṛbhir modamānau svastakau
pūrvāparaṃ carato māyaitau śiśū krīḍantau pariyāto 'rṇavam
viśvānyo bhuvanā vicaṣṭa ṛtūṃr anyo vidadhaj jāyase navaḥ
navo navo bhavasi jāyamāno 'hnāṃ ketur uṣasām eṣy agram
bhāgaṃ devebhyo vidadhāsy āyan pra candramas tirase dīrgham āyuḥ
parā dehi śāmulyaṃ brahmabhyo vibhajā vasu
kṛtyaiṣā padvatī bhūtvā jāyā viśate patim
nīlalohitaṃ bhavati kṛtyāsaktir vyajyate
edhante asyā jñātayaḥ patir bandheṣu badhyate
aślīlā tanūr bhavati ruśatī pāpayāmuyā
patir yad vadhvo vāsasaḥ svam aṅgam abhyūrṇute
āśasanaṃ viśasanam atho adhivikartanam
sūryāyāḥ paśya rūpāṇi tāni brahmota śumbhati
tṛṣṭam etat kaṭukam apāṣṭhavad viṣavan naitad attave
sūryāṃ yo brahmā veda sa id vādhūyam arhati
sa it tat syonaṃ harati brahmā vāsaḥ sumaṅgalam
prāyaścittiṃ yo adhyeti yena jāyā na riṣyati
yuvaṃ bhagaṃ saṃbharataṃ samṛddham ṛtaṃ vadantāv ṛtodyeṣu
brahmaṇaspate patim asyai rocaya cāru saṃbhalo vadatu vācam etām
ihed asātha na paro gamāthemaṃ gāvaḥ prajayā vardhayātha
śubhaṃ yatīr usriyāḥ somavarcaso viśve devāḥ krann iha vo manāṃsi
imaṃ gāvaḥ prajayā saṃviśāthāyaṃ devānāṃ na mināti bhāgam
asmai vaḥ pūṣā marutaś ca sarve asmai vo dhātā savitā suvāti
anṛkṣarā ṛjavaḥ santu panthāno yebhiḥ sakhāyo yanti no vareyam
saṃ bhagena sam aryamṇā saṃ dhātā sṛjatu varcasā
yac ca varco akṣeṣu surāyāṃ ca yad āhitam
yad goṣv aśvinā varcas tenemāṃ varcasāvatam
yena mahānagnyā jaghanam aśvinā yena vā surā
yenākṣā abhyaṣicyanta tenemāṃ varcasāvatam
yo anidhmo dīdayad apsv antar yaṃ viprāsa īḍate adhvareṣu
apāṃ napān madhumatīr apo dā yābhir indro vāvṛdhe vīryāvān
idam ahaṃ ruśantaṃ grābhaṃ tanūdūṣim apohāmi
yo bhadro rocanas tam udacāmi
āsyai brāhmaṇāḥ snapanīr harantv avīraghnīr udajantv āpaḥ
aryamṇo agniṃ paryetu pūṣan pratīkṣante śvaśuro devaraś ca
śaṃ te hiraṇyaṃ śam u santv āpaḥ śaṃ methir bhavatu śaṃ yugasya tardma
śaṃ ta āpaḥ śatapavitrā bhavantu śam u patyā tanvaṃ saṃspṛśasva
khe rathasya khe 'nasaḥ khe yugasya śatakrato
apālām indra triṣ pūtvākṛṇoḥ sūryatvacam
āśāsānā saumanasaṃ prajāṃ saubhāgyaṃ rayim
patyur anuvratā bhūtvā saṃnahyasvāmṛtāya kam
yathā sindhur nadīnāṃ sāmrājyaṃ suṣuve vṛṣā
evā tvaṃ samrājñy edhi patyur astaṃ paretya
samrājñy edhi śvaśureṣu samrājñy uta devṛṣu
nanānduḥ samrājñy edhi samrājñy uta śvaśrvāḥ
yā akṛntann avayan yāś ca tatnire yā devīr antāṁ abhito 'dadanta
tās tvā jarase saṃvyayantv āyuṣmatīdaṃ paridhatsva vāsaḥ
jīvaṃ rudanti vinayanty adhvaraṃ dīrghām anu prasitiṃ dīdhyur naraḥ
vāmaṃ pitṛbhyo ya idaṃ samīrire mayaḥ patibhyo janaye pariṣvaje
syonaṃ dhruvaṃ prajāyai dhārayāmi te 'śmānaṃ devyāḥ pṛthivyā upasthe
tam ātiṣṭhānumādyā suvarcā dīrghaṃ ta āyuḥ savitā kṛṇotu
yenāgnir asyā bhūmyā hastaṃ jagrāha dakṣiṇam
tena gṛhṇāmi te hastaṃ mā vyathiṣṭhā mayā saha prajayā ca dhanena ca
devas te savitā hastaṃ gṛhṇātu somo rājā suprajasaṃ kṛṇotu
agniḥ subhagāṃ jātavedāḥ patye patnīṃ jaradaṣṭim kṛṇotu
gṛhṇāmi te saubhagatvāya hastaṃ mayā patyā jaradaṣṭir yathāsaḥ
bhago aryamā savitā puraṃdhir mahyaṃ tvādur gārhapatyāya devāḥ
bhagas te hastam agrahīt savitā hastam agrahīt
patnī tvam asi dharmaṇāhaṃ gṛhapatis tava
mameyam astu poṣyā mahyaṃ tvādād bṛhaspatiḥ
mayā patyā prajāvati saṃjīva śaradaḥ śatam
tvaṣṭā vāso vyadadhāc chubhe kaṃ bṛhaspateḥ praśiṣā kavīnām
tenemāṃ nārīṃ savitā bhagaś ca sūryām iva paridhattāṃ prajayā
indrāgnī dyāvāpṛthivī mātariśvā mitrāvaruṇā bhago aśvinobhā
bṛhaspatir maruto brahma soma imāṃ nāriṃ prajayā vardhayantu
bṛhaspatiḥ prathamaḥ sūryāyāḥ śīrṣe keśāṁ akalpayat
tena imām aśvinā nārīm patye saṃśobhayāmasi
idaṃ tad rūpaṃ yad avasta yoṣā jāyāṃ jijñāse manasā carantīm
tām anvartiṣye sakhibhir navagvaiḥ ka imān vidvān vicacarta pāśān
ahaṃ viṣyāmi mayi rūpam asyā vedad it paśyan manasaḥ kulāyam
na steyam admi manasodamucye svayaṃ śrathnāno varuṇasya pāśān
pra tvā muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśād yena tvābadhnāt savitā suśevāḥ
uruṃ lokaṃ sugam atra panthāṃ kṛṇomi tubhyaṃ sahapatnyai vadhu
udyacchadhvam apa rakṣo hanāthemāṃ nārīṃ sukṛte dadhāta
dhātā vipaścit patim asyai viveda bhago rājā pura etu prajānan
bhagas tatakṣa caturaḥ pādān bhagas tatakṣa catvāry uṣyalāni
tvaṣṭā pipeśa madhyato 'nu vardhrānt sā no astu sumaṅgalī
sukiṃśukaṃ vahatuṃ viśvarūpaṃ hiraṇyavarṇaṃ suvṛtaṃ sucakram
āroha sūrye amṛtasya lokaṃ syonaṃ patibhyo vahatuṃ kṛṇu tvam
abhrātṛghnīṃ varuṇāpaśughnīṃ bṛhaspate
indrāpatighnīm putriṇīm āsmabhyaṃ savitar vaha
mā hiṃsiṣṭaṃ kumāryaṃ sthūṇe devakṛte pathi
śālāyā devyā dvāraṃ syonaṃ kṛṇmo vadhūpatham
brahmāparaṃ yujyatāṃ brahma pūrvaṃ brahmāntato madhyato brahma sarvataḥ
anāvyādhāṃ devapurāṃ prapadya śivā syonā patiloke virāja
tubhyam agre paryavahant sūryāṃ vahatunā saha
sa naḥ patibhyo jāyāṃ dā agne prajayā saha
punaḥ patnīm agnir adād āyuṣā saha varcasā
dīrghāyur asyā yaḥ patir jīvāti śaradaḥ śatam
somasya jāyā prathamaṃ gandharvas te 'paraḥ patiḥ
tṛtīyo agniṣ ṭe patis turīyas te manuṣyajāḥ
somo dadad gandharvāya gandharvo dadad agnaye
rayiṃ ca putrāṃś cādād agnir mahyam atho imām
ā vām agant sumatir vājinīvasū ny aśvinā hṛtsu kāmā araṃsata
abhūtaṃ gopā mithunā śubhas patī priyā aryamṇo duryāṃ aśīmahi
sā mandasānā manasā śivena rayiṃ dhehi sarvavīraṃ vacasyam
sugaṃ tīrthaṃ suprapāṇaṃ śubhas patī sthāṇuṃ pathiṣṭhām apa durmatiṃ hatam
yā oṣadhayo yā nadyo yāni kṣetrāṇi yā vanā
tās tvā vadhu prajāvatīṃ patye rakṣantu rakṣasaḥ
emaṃ panthām arukṣāma sugaṃ svastivāhanam
yasmin vīro na riṣyaty anyeṣāṃ vindate vasu
idaṃ su me naraḥ śṛṇuta yayāśiṣā daṃpatī vāmam aśnutaḥ
ye gandharvā apsarasaś ca devīr eṣu vānaspatyeṣu ye 'dhitasthuḥ
syonās te asyai vadhvai bhavantu mā hiṃsiṣur vahatum uhyamānam
ye vadhvaś candraṃ vahatuṃ yakṣmā yanti janāṁ anu
punas tān yajñiyā devā nayantu yata āgatāḥ
mā vidan paripanthino ya āsīdanti daṃpatī
sugena durgam atītām apadrāntv arātayaḥ
saṃkāśayāmi vahatuṃ brahmaṇā gṛhair aghoreṇa cakṣuṣā mitriyeṇa
paryāṇaddhaṃ viśvarūpaṃ yad asti syonaṃ patibhyaḥ savitā tat kṛṇotu
śivā nārīyam astam āgann imaṃ dhātā lokam asyai dideśa
tām aryamā bhago aśvinobhā prajāpatiḥ prajayā vardhayantu
ātmanvaty urvarā nārīyam āgan tasyāṃ naro vapata bījam asyām
sā vaḥ prajāṃ janayad vakṣaṇābhyo bibhratī dugdham ṛṣabhasya retaḥ
pratitiṣṭha virāḍ asi viṣṇur iveha sarasvati
sinīvāli prajāyatāṃ bhagasya sumatāv asat
ud va ūrmiḥ śamyā hantv āpo yoktrāṇi muñcata
māduṣkṛtau vyenasāv aghnyāv aśunam āratām
aghoracakṣur apatighnī syonā śagmā suśevā suyamā gṛhebhyaḥ
vīrasūr devṛkāmā saṃ tvayaidhiṣīmahi sumanasyamānā
adevṛghny apatighnīhaidhi śivā paśubhyaḥ suyamā suvarcāḥ
prajāvatī vīrasūr devṛkāmā syonemam agniṃ gārhapatyaṃ saparya
uttiṣṭhetaḥ kim icchantīdam āgā ahaṃ tveḍe abhibhūḥ svād gṛhāt
śūnyaiṣī nirṛte yājaganthottiṣṭhārāte prapata meha raṃsthāḥ
yadā gārhapatyam asaparyait pūrvam agniṃ vadhūr iyam
adhā sarasvatyai nāri pitṛbhyaś ca namas kuru
śarma varmaitad āharāsyai nāryā upastire
sinīvāli prajāyatāṃ bhagasya sumatāv asat
yaṃ balbajaṃ nyasyatha carma copastṛṇīthana
tad ārohatu suprajā yā kanyā vindate patim
upastṛṇīhi balbajam adhi carmaṇi rohite
tatropaviśya suprajā imam agniṃ saparyatu
āroha carmopasīdāgnim eṣa devo hanti rakṣāṃsi sarvā
iha prajāṃ janaya patye asmai sujyaiṣṭhyo bhavat putras ta eṣaḥ
vitiṣṭhantāṃ mātur asyā upasthān nānārūpāḥ paśavo jāyamānāḥ
sumaṅgaly upasīdemam agniṃ saṃpatnī pratibhūṣeha devān
sumaṅgalī prataraṇī gṛhāṇāṃ suśevā patye śvaśurāya śaṃbhūḥ
syonā śvaśrvai pra gṛhān viśemān
syonā bhava śvaśurebhyaḥ syonā patye gṛhebhyaḥ
syonāsyai sarvasyai viśe syonā puṣṭāyaiṣāṃ bhava
sumaṅgalīr iyaṃ vadhūr imāṃ sameta paśyata
saubhāgyam asyai dattvā daurbhāgyair viparetana
yā durhārdo yuvatayo yāś ceha jaratīr api
varco nv asyai saṃdattāthāstaṃ viparetana
rukmaprastaraṇaṃ vahyaṃ viśvā rūpāṇi bibhratam
ārohat sūryā sāvitrī bṛhate saubhagāya kam
āroha talpaṃ sumanasyamāneha prajāṃ janaya patye asmai
indrāṇīva subudhā budhyamānā jyotiragrā uṣasaḥ pratijāgarāsi
devā agre nyapadyanta patnīḥ samaspṛśanta tanvas tanūbhiḥ
sūryeva nāri viśvarūpā mahitvā prajāvatī patyā saṃbhaveha
uttiṣṭheto viśvāvaso namaseḍāmahe tvā
jāmim iccha pitṛṣadaṃ nyaktāṃ sa te bhāgo januṣā tasya viddhi
apsarasaḥ sadhamādaṃ madanti havirdhānam antarā sūryaṃ ca
tās te janitram abhi tāḥ parehi namas te gandharvartunā kṛṇomi
namo gandharvasya namase namo bhāmāya cakṣuṣe ca kṛṇmaḥ
viśvāvaso brahmaṇā te namo 'bhi jāyā apsarasaḥ parehi
rāyā vayaṃ sumanasaḥ syāmod ito gandharvam āvīvṛtāma
agant sa devaḥ paramaṃ sadhastham aganma yatra pratiranta āyuḥ
saṃ pitarāv ṛtviye sṛjethāṃ mātā pitā ca retaso bhavāthaḥ
marya iva yoṣām adhirohayaināṃ prajāṃ kṛṇvāthām iha puṣyataṃ rayim
tāṃ pūṣañchivatamām erayasva yasyāṃ bījaṃ manuṣyā vapanti
yā na ūrū uśatī viśrayāti yasyām uśantaḥ praharema śepaḥ
ārohorum upadhatsva hastaṃ pariṣvajasva jāyāṃ sumanasyamānaḥ
prajāṃ kṛṇvāthām iha modamānau dīrghaṃ vām āyuḥ savitā kṛṇotu
ā vāṃ prajāṃ janayatu prajāpatir ahorātrābhyāṃ samanaktv aryamā
adurmaṅgalī patilokam āviśemaṃ śaṃ no bhava dvipade śaṃ catuṣpade
devair dattaṃ manunā sākam etad vādhūyaṃ vāso vadhvaś ca vastram
yo brahmaṇe cikituṣe dadāti sa id rakṣāṃsi talpāni hanti
yaṃ me datto brahmabhāgaṃ vadhūyor vādhūyaṃ vāso vadhvaś ca vastram
yuvaṃ brahmaṇe 'numanyamānau bṛhaspate sākam indraś ca dattam
syonād yoner adhi budhyamānau hasāmudau mahasā modamānau
sugū suputrau sugṛhau tarātho jīvāv uṣaso vibhātīḥ
navaṃ vasānaḥ surabhiḥ suvāsā udāgāṃ jīva uṣaso vibhātīḥ
āṇḍāt patatrīvāmukṣi viśvasmād enasaḥ pari
śumbhanī dyāvāpṛthivī antisumne mahivrate
āpaḥ sapta susruvur devīs tā no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
sūryāyai devebhyo mitrāya varuṇāya ca
ye bhūtasya pracetasas tebhya idam akaraṃ namaḥ
ya ṛte cid abhiśriṣaḥ purā jatrubhya ātṛdaḥ
saṃdhātā saṃdhiṃ maghavā purūvasur niṣkartā vihrutaṃ punaḥ
apāsmat tama ucchatu nīlaṃ piśaṅgam uta lohitaṃ yat
nirdahanī yā pṛṣātaky asmin tāṃ sthāṇāv adhy āsajāmi
yāvatīḥ kṛtyā upavāsane yāvanto rājño varuṇasya pāśāḥ
vyṛddhayo yā asamṛddhayo yā asmin tā sthāṇāv adhi sādayāmi
yā me priyatamā tanūḥ sā me bibhāya vāsasaḥ
tasyāgre tvaṃ vanaspate nīviṃ kṛṇuṣva mā vayaṃ riṣāma
ye antā yāvatīḥ sico ya otavo ye ca tantavaḥ
vāso yat patnībhir utaṃ tan naḥ syonam upaspṛśāt
uśatīḥ kanyalā imāḥ pitṛlokāt patiṃ yatīḥ
ava dīkṣām asṛkṣata svāhā
bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan
varco goṣu praviṣṭaṃ yat tenemāṃ saṃsṛjāmasi
bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan
tejo goṣu praviṣṭaṃ yat tenemāṃ saṃsṛjāmasi
bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan
bhago goṣu praviṣṭo yas tenemāṃ saṃsṛjāmasi
bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan
yaśo goṣu praviṣṭaṃ yat tenemāṃ saṃsṛjāmasi
bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan
payo goṣu praviṣṭaṃ yat tenemāṃ saṃsṛjāmasi
bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan
raso goṣu praviṣṭo yas tenemāṃ saṃsṛjāmasi
yadīme keśino janā gṛhe te samanartiṣū rodena kṛṇvanto 'gham
agniṣ ṭvā tasmād enasaḥ savitā ca pramuñcatām
yadīyaṃ duhitā tava vikeśy arudad gṛhe rodena kṛṇvaty agham
agniṣ ṭvā tasmād enasaḥ savitā ca pramuñcatām
yaj jāmayo yad yuvatayo gṛhe te samanartiṣū rodena kṛṇvatīr agham
agniṣ ṭvā tasmād enasaḥ savitā ca pramuñcatām
yat te prajāyāṃ paśuṣu yad vā gṛheṣu niṣṭhitam aghakṛdbhir aghaṃ kṛtam
agniṣ ṭvā tasmād enasaḥ savitā ca pramuñcatām
iyaṃ nāry upabrūte pūlyāny āvapantikā
dīrghāyur astu me patir jīvāti śaradaḥ śatam
ihemāv indra saṃnuda cakravākeva daṃpatī
prajayainau svastakau viśvam āyur vyaśnutām
yad āsandyām upadhāne yad vopavāsane kṛtam
vivāhe kṛtyāṃ yāṃ cakrur āsnāne tāṃ nidadhmasi
yad duṣkṛtaṃ yac chamalaṃ vivāhe vahatau ca yat
tat saṃbhalasya kambale mṛjmahe duritaṃ vayam
saṃbhale malaṃ sādayitvā kambale duritaṃ vayam
abhūma yajñiyāḥ śuddhāḥ pra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣat
kṛtrimaḥ kaṇṭakaḥ śatadan ya eṣaḥ
apāsyāḥ keśyaṃ malam apa śīrṣaṇyaṃ likhāt
aṅgādaṅgād vayam asyā apa yakṣmaṃ nidadhmasi
tan mā prāpat pṛthivīṃ mota devān divaṃ mā prāpad urv antarikṣam
apo mā prāpan malam etad agne yamam mā prāpat pitṝṃś ca sarvān
saṃ tvā nahyāmi payasā pṛthivyāḥ saṃ tvā nahyāmi payasauṣadhīnām
saṃ tvā nahyāmi prajayā dhanena sā saṃnaddhā sanuhi vājam emam
amo 'ham asmi sā tvaṃ sāmāham asmy ṛk tvaṃ dyaur ahaṃ pṛthivī tvam
tāv iha saṃbhavāva prajām ājanayāvahai
janiyanti nāv agravaḥ putriyanti sudānavaḥ
ariṣṭāsū sacevahi bṛhate vājasātaye
ye pitaro vadhūdarśā imaṃ vahatum āgaman
te asyai vadhvai saṃpatnyai prajāvaccharma yacchantu
yedaṃ pūrvāgan raśanāyamānā prajām asyai draviṇaṃ ceha dattvā
tāṃ vahantv agatasyānu panthāṃ virāḍ iyaṃ suprajā atyajaiṣīt
prabudhyasva subudhā budhyamānā dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya
gṛhān gaccha gṛhapatnī yathāso dīrghaṃ ta āyuḥ savitā kṛṇotu
vrātyaḥ āsīt īyamānaḥ eva
sa prajāpatim samairayat
sa prajāpatiḥ suvarṇam ātman apaśyat
tat prājanayat
tat ekam abhavat
tat lalāmam abhavat
tat mahat abhavat
tat jyeṣṭham abhavat
tat brahma abhavat
tat tapaḥ abhavat
tat satyam abhavat
tena prājāyata
saḥ avardhata
sa mahān abhavat
sa mahādevaḥ abhavat
sa devānām īśām paryait
saḥ īśānaḥ abhavat
saḥ eka vrātyaḥ abhavat
sa dhanuḥ ādatta
tat eva indra dhanuḥ
nīlam asya udaram
lohitam pṛṣṭham
nīlena eva apriyam bhrātṛvyam prorṇoti lohitena dviṣantam vidhyati iti brahma vādinaḥ vadanti
saḥ udatiṣṭhat
sa prācīm diśam anuvyacalat
tam bṛhat ca rathantaram ca ādityāḥ ca viśve ca devāḥ anuvyacalan
bṛhate ca vai sa rathantarāya ca ādityebhyaḥ ca viśvebhyaḥ ca devebhyaḥ āvṛścate yaḥ evam vidvāṃsam vrātyam upavadati
bṛhataḥ ca vai sa rathantarasya ca ādityānām ca viśveṣām ca devānām priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
śraddhā
tasya prācyām diśi śraddhā puṃścalī mitraḥ māgadhaḥ vijñānam vāsaḥ ahar uṣṇīṣam rātrī keśāḥ haritau pravartau kalmaliḥ maṇiḥ bhūtam ca bhaviṣyat ca pariṣkandau manaḥ vipatham mātariśvā ca pavamānaḥ ca vipatha vāhau vātaḥ sārathiḥ reṣmā pratodaḥ kīrtiḥ ca yaśaḥ ca puraḥsarau
ā enam kīrtiḥ gacchati ā yaśaḥ gacchati yaḥ evam veda
saḥ udatiṣṭhat
sa dakṣiṇām diśam anuvyacalat
tam yajñāyajñiyam ca vāmadevyam ca yajñaḥ ca yajamānaḥ ca paśavaḥ ca anuvyacalan
yajñāyajñiyāya ca sa vāmadevyāya ca yajñāya ca yajamānāya ca paśubhyaḥ ca āvṛścate yaḥ evam vidvāṃsam vrātyam upavadati
yajñāyajñiyasya ca vai sa vāmadevyasya ca yajñasya ca yajamānasya ca paśūnām ca priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
uṣāḥ
tasya dakṣiṇāyām diśi uṣāḥ puṃścalī mantraḥ māgadhaḥ vijñānam vāsaḥ ahar uṣṇīṣam rātrī keśāḥ haritau pravartau kalmaliḥ maṇiḥ amāvāsyā ca paurṇamāsī ca pariṣkandau manaḥ vipatham mātariśvā ca pavamānaḥ ca vipatha vāhau vātaḥ sārathiḥ reṣmā pratodaḥ kīrtiḥ ca yaśaḥ ca puraḥsarau
ā enam kīrtiḥ gacchati ā yaśaḥ gacchati yaḥ evam veda
saḥ udatiṣṭhat
sa pratīcīm diśam anuvyacalat
tam anuvyacalan
vairūpāya ca vai sa vairājāya ca adbhyaḥ ca varuṇāya ca rājñe āvṛścate yaḥ evam vidvāṃsam vrātyam upavadati
vairūpasya ca vai sa vairājasya ca apām ca varuṇasya ca rājñaḥ priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
irā
tasya pratīcyām diśi irā puṃścalī hasaḥ māgadhaḥ vijñānam vāsaḥ ahar uṣṇīṣam rātrī keśāḥ haritau pravartau kalmaliḥ maṇiḥ ahar ca rātrī ca pariṣkandau manaḥ vipatham mātariśvā ca pavamānaḥ ca vipatha vāhau vātaḥ sārathiḥ reṣmā pratodaḥ kīrtiḥ ca yaśaḥ ca puraḥsarau
ā enam kīrtiḥ gacchati ā yaśaḥ gacchati yaḥ evam veda
saḥ udatiṣṭhat
saḥ udīcīm diśam anuvyacalat
tam śyaitam ca naudhasam ca saptarṣayaḥ ca somaḥ ca rājā anuvyacalan
śyaitāya ca vai sa naudhasāya ca saptarṣibhyaḥ ca somāya ca rājñe āvṛścate yaḥ evam vidvāṃsam vrātyam upavadati
śyaitasya ca vai sa naudhasasya ca saptarṣīṇām ca somasya ca rājñaḥ priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
vidyut
tasya udīcyām diśi vidyut puṃścalī stanayitnuḥ māgadhaḥ vijñānam vāsaḥ ahar uṣṇīṣam rātrī keśāḥ haritau pravartau kalmaliḥ maṇiḥ śrutam ca viśrutam ca pariṣkandau manaḥ vipatham mātariśvā ca pavamānaḥ ca vipatha vāhau vātaḥ sārathiḥ reṣmā pratodaḥ kīrtiḥ ca yaśaḥ ca puraḥsarau
ā enam kīrtiḥ gacchati ā yaśaḥ gacchati yaḥ evam veda
sa saṃvatsaram ūrdhvaḥ atiṣṭhat
tam devāḥ abruvan vrātya kim nu tiṣṭhasi iti
saḥ abravīt āsandīm me saṃbharantu iti
tasmai vrātyāya āsandīm samabharan
tasyāḥ grīṣmaḥ ca vasantaḥ ca dvau pādau āstām śarad ca varṣāḥ ca dvau
bṛhat ca rathantaram ca anūcye āstām yajñāyajñiyam ca vāmadevyam ca tiraścye
ṛcaḥ prāñcaḥ tantavaḥ yajūṃṣi tiryañcaḥ
vedaḥ āstaraṇam brahma upabarhaṇam
sāma āsādaḥ udgīthaḥ apaśrayaḥ
tām āsandīm vrātyaḥ ārohat
tasya deva janāḥ pariṣkandāḥ āsan saṃkalpāḥ prahāyyāḥ viśvāni bhūtāni upasadaḥ
viśvāni eva asya bhūtāni upasadaḥ bhavanti yaḥ evam veda
tasmai prācyāḥ diśaḥ vāsantau māsau goptārau akurvan bṛhat ca rathantaram ca anuṣṭhātārau
vāsantau enam māsau prācyāḥ diśaḥ gopāyataḥ bṛhat ca rathantaram ca anutiṣṭhataḥ yaḥ evam veda
tasmai dakṣiṇāyāḥ diśaḥ graiṣmau māsau goptārau akurvan yajñāyajñiyam ca vāmadevyam ca anuṣṭhātārau
graiṣmau enam māsau dakṣiṇāyāḥ diśaḥ gopāyataḥ yajñāyajñiyam ca vāmadevyam ca anutiṣṭhataḥ yaḥ evam veda
tasmai pratīcyāḥ diśaḥ vārṣikau māsau goptārau akurvan vairūpam ca vairājam ca anuṣṭhātārau
vārṣikau enam māsau pratīcyāḥ diśaḥ gopāyataḥ vairūpam ca vairājam ca anutiṣṭhataḥ yaḥ evam veda
tasmai udīcyāḥ diśaḥ śāradau māsau goptārau akurvan śyaitam ca naudhasam ca anuṣṭhātārau
śāradau enam māsau udīcyāḥ diśaḥ gopāyataḥ śyaitam ca naudhasam ca anutiṣṭhataḥ yaḥ evam veda
tasmai dhruvāyāḥ diśaḥ haimanau māsau goptārau akurvan bhūmim ca agnim ca anuṣṭhātārau
haimanau enam māsau dhruvāyāḥ diśaḥ gopāyataḥ bhūmiḥ ca agniḥ ca anutiṣṭhataḥ yaḥ evam veda
tasmai ūrdhvāyāḥ diśaḥ śaiśirau māsau goptārau akurvan divam ca ādityam ca anuṣṭhātārau
śaiśirau enam māsau ūrdhvāyāḥ diśaḥ gopāyataḥ dyauḥ ca ādityaḥ ca anutiṣṭhataḥ yaḥ evam veda
tasmai prācyāḥ diśaḥ antardeśāt bhavam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
bhavaḥ enam iṣvāsaḥ prācyāḥ diśaḥ antardeśāt anuṣṭhātā anutiṣṭhati
na enam śarvaḥ na bhavaḥ na īśānaḥ na asya paśūn na samānān hinasti yaḥ evam veda
tasmai dakṣiṇāyāḥ diśaḥ antardeśāt śarvam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
śarvaḥ enam iṣvāsaḥ dakṣiṇāyāḥ diśaḥ antardeśāt anuṣṭhātā anutiṣṭhati
na enam śarvaḥ na bhavaḥ na īśānaḥ na asya paśūn na samānān hinasti yaḥ evam veda
tasmai pratīcyāḥ diśaḥ antardeśāt paśupatim iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
paśupatiḥ enam iṣvāsaḥ pratīcyāḥ diśaḥ antardeśāt anuṣṭhātā anutiṣṭhati
na enam śarvaḥ na bhavaḥ na īśānaḥ na asya paśūn na samānān hinasti yaḥ evam veda
tasmai udīcyāḥ diśaḥ antardeśāt ugram devam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
ugraḥ enam devaḥ iṣvāsaḥ udīcyāḥ diśaḥ antardeśāt anuṣṭhātā anutiṣṭhati
na enam śarvaḥ na bhavaḥ na īśānaḥ na asya paśūn na samānān hinasti yaḥ evam veda
tasmai dhruvāyāḥ diśaḥ antardeśāt rudram iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
rudraḥ enam iṣvāsaḥ dhruvāyāḥ diśaḥ antardeśāt anuṣṭhātā anutiṣṭhati
na enam śarvaḥ na bhavaḥ na īśānaḥ na asya paśūn na samānān hinasti yaḥ evam veda
tasmai ūrdhvāyāḥ diśaḥ antardeśāt mahādevam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
mahādevaḥ enam iṣvāsaḥ ūrdhvāyāḥ diśaḥ antardeśāt anuṣṭhātā anutiṣṭhati
na enam śarvaḥ na bhavaḥ na īśānaḥ na asya paśūn na samānān hinasti yaḥ evam veda
tasmai sarvebhyaḥ antardeśebhyaḥ īśānam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
īśānaḥ enam iṣvāsaḥ sarvebhyaḥ antardeśebhyaḥ anuṣṭhātā anutiṣṭhati
na enam śarvaḥ na bhavaḥ na īśānaḥ na asya paśūn na samānān hinasti yaḥ evam veda
sa dhruvām diśam anuvyacalat
tam bhūmiḥ ca agniḥ ca oṣadhayaḥ ca vanaspatayaḥ ca vānaspatyāḥ ca vīrudhaḥ ca anuvyacalan
bhūmeḥ ca vai saḥ agneḥ ca oṣadhīnām ca vanaspatīnām ca vānaspatyānām ca vīrudhām ca priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
saḥ ūrdhvām diśam anuvyacalat
tam ṛtam ca satyam ca sūryaḥ ca candraḥ ca nakṣatrāṇi ca anuvyacalan
ṛtasya ca vai sa satyasya ca sūryasya ca candrasya ca nakṣatrāṇām ca priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
saḥ uttamām diśam anuvyacalat
tam ṛcaḥ ca sāmāni ca yajūṃṣi ca brahma ca anuvyacalan
ṛcām ca vai sa sāmnām ca yajuṣām ca brahmaṇaḥ ca priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
sa bṛhatīm diśam anuvyacalat
tam itihāsaḥ ca purāṇam ca gāthāḥ ca nārāśaṃsīḥ ca anuvyacalan
itihāsasya ca vai sa purāṇasya ca gāthānām ca nārāśaṃsīnām ca priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
sa paramām diśam anuvyacalat
tam āhavanīyaḥ ca gārhapatyaḥ ca dakṣiṇāgniḥ ca yajñaḥ ca yajamānaḥ ca paśavaḥ ca anuvyacalan
āhavanīyasya ca vai sa gārhapatyasya ca dakṣiṇāgneḥ ca yajñasya ca yajamānasya ca paśūnām ca priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
saḥ an ādiṣṭām diśam anuvyacalat
tam ṛtavaḥ ca ārtavāḥ ca lokāḥ ca laukyāḥ ca māsāḥ ca ardha māsāḥ ca ahorātre ca anuvyacalan
ṛtūnām ca vai saḥ ārtavānām ca lokānām ca laukyānām ca māsānām ca ardha māsānām ca ahorātrayoḥ ca priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
saḥ an āvṛttām diśam anuvyacalat
tatas na āvartsyan amanyata
tam ditiḥ ca aditiḥ ca iḍā ca indrāṇī ca anuvyacalan
diteḥ ca vai saḥ aditeḥ ca iḍāyāḥ ca indrāṇyāḥ ca priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
sa diśaḥ anuvyacalat
tam virāj anuvyacalat sarve ca devāḥ sarvāḥ ca devatāḥ
virājaḥ ca vai sa sarveṣām ca devānām sarvāsām ca devatānām priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
sa sarvān antardeśān anuvyacalat
tam prajāpatiḥ ca parameṣṭhī ca pitā ca pitāmahaḥ ca anuvyacalan
prajāpateḥ ca vai sa parameṣṭhinaḥ ca pituḥ ca pitāmahasya ca priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
sa mahimā sadruḥ bhūtvā antam pṛthivyāḥ agacchat
samudraḥ abhavat
tam prajāpatiḥ ca parameṣṭhī ca pitā ca pitāmahaḥ ca apaḥ ca śraddhā ca varṣam bhūtvā anuvyavartayanta
ā enam āpaḥ gacchanti ā enam śraddhā gacchati ā enam varṣam gacchati yaḥ evam veda
tam śraddhā ca yajñaḥ ca lokaḥ ca annam ca annādyam ca bhūtvā abhiparyāvartanta
ā enam śraddhā gacchati ā enam yajñaḥ gacchati ā enam lokaḥ gacchati ā enam annam gacchati ā enam annādyam gacchati yaḥ evam veda
saḥ arajyata
tatas rājanyaḥ ajāyata
sa viśaḥ sabandhūn annam annādyam abhyudatiṣṭhat
viśām ca vai sa sabandhūnām ca annasya ca annādyasya ca priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
sa viśaḥ anuvyacalat
tam sabhā ca samitiḥ ca senā ca surā ca anuvyacalan
sabhāyāḥ ca vai sa samiteḥ ca senāyāḥ ca surāyāḥ ca priyam dhāma bhavati yaḥ evam veda
tat yasya evam vidvān vrātyaḥ rājñaḥ atithiḥ gṛhān āgacchet śreyāṃsam enam ātmanaḥ mānayet
tathā kṣatrāya na āvṛścate
tathā rāṣṭrāya na āvṛścate
atas vai brahma ca kṣatram ca udatiṣṭhatām
te abrūtām kam praviśāva iti
bṛhaspatim eva brahma praviśatu indram kṣatram
tathā vai iti
atas vai bṛhaspatim eva brahma prāviśat indram kṣatram
iyam vai u pṛthivī bṛhaspatiḥ
dyauḥ eva indraḥ
ayam vai u agniḥ brahma
asau ādityaḥ kṣatram
ā enam brahma gacchati brahmavarcasī bhavati yaḥ pṛthivīm bṛhaspatim agnim brahma veda
ā enam indriyam gacchati indriyavān bhavati yaḥ ādityam kṣatram divam indram veda
tat yasya evam vidvān vrātyaḥ atithiḥ gṛhān āgacchet svayam enam abhyudetya brūyāt vrātya kva avātsīḥ vrātya udakam vrātya tarpayantu vrātya yathā te priyam tathā astu vrātya yathā te vaśaḥ tathā astu vrātya yathā te nikāmaḥ tathā astu iti
yat enam āha vrātya kva avātsīḥ iti pathaḥ eva tena deva yānān avarunddhe
yat enam āha vrātya udakam iti apaḥ eva tena avarunddhe
yat enam āha vrātya tarpayantu iti prāṇam eva tena varṣīyāṃsam kurute
yat enam āha vrātya yathā te priyam tathā astu iti priyam eva tena avarunddhe
ā enam priyam gacchati priyaḥ priyasya bhavati yaḥ evam veda
yat enam āha vrātya yathā te vaśaḥ tathā astu iti vaśam eva tena avarunddhe
ā enam vaśaḥ gacchati vaśī vaśinām bhavati yaḥ evam veda
yat enam āha vrātya yathā te nikāmaḥ tathā astu iti nikāmam eva tena avarunddhe
ā enam nikāmaḥ gacchati nikāme nikāmasya bhavati yaḥ evam veda
tat yasya evam vidvān vrātyaḥ uddhṛteṣu agniṣu adhiśrite agnihotre atithiḥ gṛhān āgacchet svayam enam abhyudetya brūyāt vrātya atisṛja hoṣyāmi iti
sa ca atisṛjet juhuyāt
na ca atisṛjet na juhuyāt
sa yaḥ evam viduṣā vrātyena atisṛṣṭaḥ juhoti pra pitṛyāṇam panthām jānāti pra deva yānam
na deveṣu āvṛścate
hutam asya bhavati
pari asya asmin loke āyatanam śiṣyate yaḥ evam viduṣā vrātyena atisṛṣṭaḥ juhoti
atha yaḥ evam viduṣā vrātyena an atisṛṣṭaḥ juhoti na pitṛyāṇam panthām jānāti na deva yānam
ā deveṣu vṛścate
ahutam asya bhavati
na asya asmin loke āyatanam śiṣyate yaḥ evam viduṣā vrātyena an atisṛṣṭaḥ juhoti
tat yasya evam vidvān vrātyaḥ ekām rātrim atithiḥ gṛhe vasati ye pṛthivyām puṇyāḥ lokāḥ tān eva tena avarunddhe
tat yasya evam vidvān vrātyaḥ dvitīyām rātrim atithiḥ gṛhe vasati ye antarikṣe puṇyāḥ lokāḥ tān eva tena avarunddhe
tat yasya evam vidvān vrātyaḥ tṛtīyām rātrim atithiḥ gṛhe vasati ye divi puṇyāḥ lokāḥ tān eva tena avarunddhe
tat yasya evam vidvān vrātyaḥ caturthīm rātrim atithiḥ gṛhe vasati ye puṇyānām puṇyāḥ lokāḥ tān eva tena avarunddhe
tat yasya evam vidvān vrātyaḥ aparimitāḥ rātrīḥ atithiḥ gṛhe vasati ye eva aparimitāḥ puṇyāḥ lokāḥ tān eva tena avarunddhe
atha yasya avrātyaḥ vrātya bruvaḥ nāmabibhratī atithiḥ gṛhān āgacchet karṣet enam na ca enam karṣet
asyai devatāyai udakam yācāmi imām devatām vāsaye imām imām devatām pariveveṣmi iti enam pariveviṣyāt
tasyām eva asya tat devatāyām hutam bhavati yaḥ evam veda
sa yat prācīm diśam anuvyacalat mārutam śardhaḥ bhūtvā anuvyacalat manaḥ anna ādam kṛtvā
manasā anna ādena annam atti yaḥ evam veda
sa yat dakṣiṇām diśam anuvyacalat indraḥ bhūtvā anuvyacalat balam anna ādam kṛtvā
balena anna ādena annam atti yaḥ evam veda
sa yat pratīcīm diśam anuvyacalat varuṇaḥ rājā bhūtvā anuvyacalat apaḥ annādīḥ kṛtvā
adbhiḥ annādībhiḥ annam atti yaḥ evam veda
sa yat udīcīm diśam anuvyacalat somaḥ rājā bhūtvā anuvyacalat saptarṣibhiḥ hute āhutim annādīm kṛtvā
āhutyā annādyā annam atti yaḥ evam veda
sa yat dhruvām diśam anuvyacalat viṣṇuḥ bhūtvā anuvyacalat virājam annādīm kṛtvā
virājā annādyā annam atti yaḥ evam veda
sa yat paśūn anuvyacalat rudraḥ bhūtvā anuvyacalat oṣadhīḥ annādīḥ kṛtvā
oṣadhībhiḥ annādībhiḥ annam atti yaḥ evam veda
sa yat pitṝn anuvyacalat yamaḥ rājā bhūtvā anuvyacalat svadhākāram anna ādam kṛtvā
svadhākāreṇa annādena annam atti yaḥ evam veda
sa yat manuṣyān anuvyacalat agniḥ bhūtvā anuvyacalat svāhākāram anna ādam kṛtvā
svāhākāreṇa anna ādena annam atti yaḥ evam veda
sa yat ūrdhvām diśam anuvyacalat bṛhaspatiḥ bhūtvā anuvyacalat vaṣaṭkāram anna ādam kṛtvā
vaṣaṭkāreṇa anna ādena annam atti yaḥ evam veda
sa yat devān anuvyacalat īśānaḥ bhūtvā anuvyacalat manyum anna ādam kṛtvā
manyunā anna ādena annam atti yaḥ evam veda
sa yat prajāḥ anuvyacalat prajāpatiḥ bhūtvā anuvyacalat prāṇam anna ādam kṛtvā
prāṇena anna ādena annam atti yaḥ evam veda
sa yat sarvān antardeśān anuvyacalat parameṣṭhī bhūtvā anuvyacalat brahma anna ādam kṛtvā
brahmaṇā anna ādena annam atti yaḥ evam veda
tasya vrātyasya sapta prāṇāḥ sapta apānāḥ sapta vyānāḥ
yaḥ asya prathamaḥ prāṇaḥ ūrdhvaḥ nāma ayam saḥ agniḥ
yaḥ asya dvitīyaḥ prāṇaḥ prauḍhaḥ nāma asau saḥ ādityaḥ
yaḥ asya tṛtīyaḥ prāṇaḥ abhyūḍhaḥ nāma asau sa candramāḥ
yaḥ asya caturthaḥ prāṇaḥ vibhūḥ nāma ayam sa pavamānaḥ
yaḥ asya pañcamaḥ prāṇaḥ yoniḥ nāma tāḥ imāḥ āpaḥ
yaḥ asya ṣaṣṭhaḥ prāṇaḥ priyaḥ nāma te ime paśavaḥ
yaḥ asya saptamaḥ prāṇaḥ aparimitaḥ nāma tāḥ imāḥ prajāḥ
yaḥ asya prathamaḥ apānaḥ sā paurṇamāsī
yaḥ asya dvitīyaḥ apānaḥ sā aṣṭakā
yaḥ asya tṛtīyaḥ apānaḥ sā amāvāsyā
yaḥ asya caturthaḥ apānaḥ sā śraddhā
yaḥ asya pañcamaḥ apānaḥ sā dīkṣā
yaḥ asya ṣaṣṭhaḥ apānaḥ sa yajñaḥ
yaḥ asya saptamaḥ apānaḥ tāḥ imāḥ dakṣiṇāḥ
yaḥ asya prathamaḥ vyānaḥ sā iyam bhūmiḥ
yaḥ asya dvitīyaḥ vyānaḥ tat antarikṣam
yaḥ asya tṛtīyaḥ vyānaḥ sā dyauḥ
yaḥ asya caturthaḥ vyānaḥ tāni nakṣatrāṇi
yaḥ asya pañcamaḥ vyānaḥ te ṛtavaḥ
yaḥ asya ṣaṣṭhaḥ vyānaḥ te ārtavāḥ
yaḥ asya saptamaḥ vyānaḥ sa saṃvatsaraḥ
samānam artham pariyanti devāḥ
saṃvatsaram vai etat ṛtavaḥ anupariyanti vrātyam ca
yat ādityam abhisaṃviśanti amāvāsyām ca eva tat paurṇamāsīm ca
tat
ekam tat eṣām amṛta tvam
iti āhutiḥ eva
tasya vrātyasya
yat asya dakṣiṇam akṣi asau saḥ ādityaḥ
yat asya savyam akṣi asau sa candramāḥ
yaḥ asya dakṣiṇaḥ karṇaḥ ayam saḥ agniḥ
yaḥ asya savyaḥ karṇaḥ ayam sa pavamānaḥ
ahorātre nāsike
ditiḥ ca aditiḥ ca śīrṣa kapāle
saṃvatsaraḥ śiraḥ
ahnā pratyaṅ vrātyaḥ rātryā prāṅ
namaḥ vrātyāya
atisṛṣṭaḥ apām vṛṣabhaḥ
atisṛṣṭāḥ agnayaḥ divyāḥ rujan parirujan mṛṇan pramṛṇan mrokaḥ manaḥ hā khanaḥ nirdāhaḥ ātma dūṣiḥ tanū dūṣiḥ
idam tam atisṛjāmi
tam mā abhyavanikṣi
tena tam abhyatisṛjāmaḥ yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam vayam dviṣmaḥ
apām agram asi
samudram vaḥ abhyavasṛjāmi
yaḥ apsu agniḥ ati tam sṛjāmi mrokam khanim tanū dūṣim
yaḥ vaḥ āpaḥ agniḥ āviveśa saḥ eṣa
yat vaḥ ghoram tat etat
indrasya vaḥ indriyeṇa abhiṣiñcet
ariprāḥ āpaḥ
apa ripram asmat
pra asmat enaḥ vahantu
pra duṣvapnyam vahantu
śivena mā cakṣuṣā paśyata apaḥ
śivayā tanvā upaspṛśata tvacam me
śivān agnīn apsuṣadaḥ havāmahe
mayi kṣatram varcaḥ ādhatta devīḥ
nir durarmaṇya ūrjā madhumatī vāk
madhumatī stha madhumatīṃ vācam udeyam
upahūto me gopāḥ upahūto gopīthaḥ
suśrutau karṇau bhadraśrutau karṇau bhadraṃ ślokaṃ śrūyāsam
suśrutiś ca mopaśrutiś ca mā hāsiṣṭāṃ sauparṇaṃ cakṣur ajasraṃ jyotiḥ
ṛṣīṇāṃ prastaro 'si namo 'stu daivāya prastarāya
mūrdhā aham rayīṇām mūrdhā samānānām bhūyāsam
rujaḥ ca mā venaḥ ca mā hāsiṣṭām
mūrdhā ca mā vidharmā ca mā hāsiṣṭām
urvaḥ ca mā camasaḥ ca mā hāsiṣṭām
dhartā ca mā dharuṇaḥ ca mā hāsiṣṭām
vimokaḥ ca mā ārdra paviḥ ca mā hāsiṣṭām
ārdra dānuḥ ca mā mātariśvā ca mā hāsiṣṭām
bṛhaspatiḥ me ātmā nṛmaṇāḥ nāma hṛdyaḥ
a saṃtāpam me hṛdayam
urvī gavyūtiḥ
samudraḥ asmi vidharmaṇā
nābhiḥ aham rayīṇām nābhiḥ samānānām bhūyāsam
svāsad asi sūṣāḥ amṛtaḥ martyeṣu ā
mā mām prāṇaḥ hāsīt mā u apānaḥ avahāya parāgāt
sūryaḥ mā ahnaḥ pātu agniḥ pṛthivyāḥ vāyuḥ antarikṣāt yamaḥ manuṣyebhyaḥ sarasvatī pārthivebhyaḥ
prāṇa apānau mā mā hāsiṣṭam
mā jane prameṣi
svasti adya uṣasaḥ ca sarvaḥ āpaḥ sarva gaṇaḥ aśīya
śakvarīḥ stha
paśavaḥ mā upastheṣuḥ
mitrāvaruṇau me prāṇa apānau agniḥ me dakṣam dadhātu
vidma te svapna janitraṃ grāhyāḥ putro 'si yamasya karaṇaḥ
antako 'si mṛtyur asi
taṃ tvā svapna tathā saṃvidma sa naḥ svapna duṣvapnyāt pāhi
vidma te svapna janitraṃ nirṛtyāḥ putro 'si yamasya karaṇaḥ
vidma te svapna janitraṃ abhūtyāḥ putro 'si yamasya karaṇaḥ
vidma te svapna janitraṃ nirbhūtyāḥ putro 'si yamasya karaṇaḥ
vidma te svapna janitraṃ parābhūtyāḥ putro 'si yamasya karaṇaḥ
vidma te svapna janitraṃ devajāmīnāṃ putro 'si yamasya karaṇaḥ
antako 'si mṛtyur asi
taṃ tvā svapna tathā saṃvidma sa naḥ svapna duṣvapnyāt pāhi
ajaiṣmādyāsanāmādyābhūmānāgaso vayam
uṣo yasmād duṣvapnyād abhaiṣmāpa tad ucchatu
dviṣate tat parāvaha śapate tat parāvaha
yaṃ dviṣmo yaś ca no dveṣṭi tasmā enad gamayāmaḥ
uṣā devī vācā saṃvidānā vāg devy uṣasā saṃvidānā
uṣaspatir vācaspatinā saṃvidāno vācaspatir uṣaspatinā saṃvidānaḥ
te 'muṣmai parāvahantv arāyān durṇāmnaḥ sadānvāḥ
kumbhīkāḥ dūṣīkāḥ pīyakān
jāgradduṣvapnyaṃ svapne duṣvapnyam
anāgamiṣyato varān avitteḥ saṃkalpān amucyā druhaḥ pāśān
tad amuṣmā agne devāḥ parāvahantu vadhrir yathāsad vithuro na sādhuḥ
tenainaṃ vidhyāmy abhūtyainaṃ vidhyāmi nirbhūtyainaṃ vidhyāmi parābhūtyainaṃ vidhyāmi grāhyainaṃ vidhyāmi tamasainaṃ vidhyāmi
devānām enaṃ ghoraiḥ krūraiḥ praiṣair abhipreṣyāmi
vaiśvānarasyainaṃ daṃṣṭrayor apidadhāmi
evānevāva sā garat
yo 'smān dveṣṭi tam ātmā dveṣṭu yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ sa ātmānaṃ dveṣṭu
nir dviṣantaṃ divo niḥ pṛthivyā nir antarikṣād bhajāma
suyāmaṃś cākṣuṣa
idam aham āmuṣyāyaṇe 'muṣyāḥ putre duṣvapnyaṃ mṛje
yad ado ado abhyagacchaṃ yad doṣā yat pūrvāṃ rātrim
yaj jāgrad yat supto yad divā yan naktam
yad aharahar abhigacchāmi tasmād enam avadaye
taṃ jahi tena mandasva tasya pṛṣṭīr apiśṛṇīhi
sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāṇo jahātu
jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam ṛtam asmākaṃ tejo 'smākaṃ brahmāsmākaṃ svar asmākaṃ yajño 'smākaṃ paśavo 'smākaṃ prajā asmākaṃ vīrā asmākam
tasmāt amum nirbhajāmaḥ amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram asau yaḥ
sa grāhyāḥ pāśāt mā moci
tasya idam varcaḥ tejaḥ prāṇam āyuḥ nirveṣṭayāmi
idam enam adharāñcam pādayāmi
jitam asmākam ﾰ
saḥ nirṛtyāḥ pāśāt mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
saḥ abhūtyāḥ pāśāt mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa nirbhūtyāḥ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa parābhūtyāḥ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa devajāmīnāṃ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa bṛhaspateḥ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa prajāpateḥ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa ṛṣīṇāṃ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa ārṣeyāṇāṃ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
so 'ṅgirasāṃ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa āṅgirasānāṃ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
so 'tharvaṇām pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa ātharvaṇānāṃ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa vanaspatīṇāṃ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa vānaspatyānāṃ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa ṛtūnāṃ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa ārtavānāṃ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa māsānāṃ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
so 'rdhamāsānāṃ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
so 'horātrayoḥ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
so 'hnoḥ saṃyatoḥ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa indrāgnyoḥ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa mitrāvaruṇayoḥ pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa rājño varuṇasya pāśān mā moci
jitam asmākam ﾰ
sa mṛtyoḥ paḍvīśāt pāśānmā moci
jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam abhyaṣṭhāṃ viśvāḥ pṛtanā arātīḥ
tad agnir āha tad u soma āha pūṣā mā dhāt sukṛtasya loke
aganma svaḥ svar aganma saṃ sūryasya jyotiṣāganma

priyaḥ devānām bhūyāsam
viṣāsahim sahamānam sāsahānam sahīyāṃsam sahamānam sahaḥ jitam svar jitam go jitam saṃdhanājitam īḍyam nāma hve indram
priyaḥ prajānām bhūyāsam
viṣāsahim sahamānam sāsahānam sahīyāṃsam sahamānam sahaḥ jitam svar jitam go jitam saṃdhanājitam īḍyam nāma hve indram
priyaḥ paśūnām bhūyāsam
viṣāsahim sahamānam sāsahānam sahīyāṃsam sahamānam sahaḥ jitam svar jitam go jitam saṃdhanājitam īḍyam nāma hve indram
